商業新聞證劵逸出常軌的債市　　市價漲跌瞬息萬變　　三盤成交近四千萬　　昨華商證劵交易所、市價趨勢、至爲奇特、波瀾起伏、瞬息萬變、有令人目迷五色之槪、謡言亦隨之而起滅無常、足見人心之恍惚、實有忐忑不安之狀、其實謡言殊屬無稽、而市上大多頭逢高出簡事實有之、故市價漲跌、極爲迅速、此種狀態、亦係逼近交割時、有以致之、前途趨勢、仍有反復也、昨日交易、共做三盤、收盤時已逾七時、足見交易之踴躍、畸形發展、方興未艾、昨日開盤、人心甚堅、大致一致趨漲、數角至一元餘、但自統税遠期起、又趨疲軟、反小一二角至半元、前後趨勢、背道而馳、人心又復轉下、次盤一瀉數角至一元六角之多、可見多頭逢高出籠、以求生路、午後紙做一盤、開盤時已將六時、多頭暫止售出、各帮又有抬價形勢、再轉漲風、漲一元左右、變化之迅速、漲跌之離奇、實已不合常軌、最近數日内、當仍不脱此現象也、市價結果、計漲跌互見、大致前列至廿捲止、略好二三角餘均小三五六角不等、成交總數、仍在四千萬元之譜、時遲不及詳舉、茲將其漲跌結果、列比較表於左、種　類　期貨　最　　　高　最　　　低　較　前　週一八關　八月　二九·四○　二八·九○　漲○·○五編　遣　八月　四三·五○　四二·九○　又○·三○又　　　九月　四三·三五　四二·五五　又○·○五裁　兵　八月　七六·七○　七五·六○　又○·三五又　　　九月　七七·八○　七六·一五　又○·三五一九關　八月　四五·五五　四四·五○　又○·○五又　　　九月　四四·九○　四四·○○　又○·一五一九善　八月　五一·一○　四九·九五　跌○·三五又　　　九月　五○·三○　四九·一○　漲○·二○廿　捲　八月　五四·四○　五三·四○　又○·三五又　　　九月　五四·一五　五二·八○　又○·一五廿　關　八月　五五·七五　五三·七○　跌○·七○又　　　九月　五五·○五　五三·六○　又○·二○廿　統　八月　五八·七○　五七·一○　又○·五五又　　　九月　五八·○○　五六·六五　又○·三○廿　鹽　八月　五九·三○　五八·○○　又○·六○又　　　九月　五八·九○　五七·八○　又○·三五金　短　八月　七四·七○　七二·七○　又○·五五又　　　九月　七四·○五　七三·五○　又○·二○二二關　八月　六五·二五　六四·三○　又○·二五又　　　九月　六四·九五　六三·九○　又○·三○二三關　八月　七三·九○　七三·五○　又○·二五又　　　九月　七三·二五　七二·四○　又○·二○整　六　八月　六九·四五　六八·五○　又○·一五又　　　九月　六八·四○　六七·一○　漲○·二五九　六　八月　一二·三五　一二·○○　不　　　動九　六　九月　一二·五○　一二·○五　跌○·五○金　長　八月　五一·○○　五○·五○　漲○·六○紐約農業區鐵道股獨挺　　新豐洋行報告、昨（二十一日）紐約證券交易所市面、人心轉堅、農業區之鐵道尤挺、糖股因古巴商約消息良好而漲、農具郵售商店與肥料等股則以雜糧進步、價亦上升、小交易所交易甚清、然因礦股升起、市面亦堅、希倫華格之需要頗殷、致酒股空頭亟起補進、債市先因美政府公債軟弱而生動摇、旋即回漲、步驟不整、芝加哥小麥市塲、散户交易頗湧、經紀商之了結爲公衆所吸收、全日成交五十八萬股、道瓊斯指數如左　　　　　　　二十日　　　二十一日　　上落三十種實業股　九○·四四　九二·五七　漲二·一三二十種鐵道股　三四·五四　三五·六八　漲一·一四二十種公用股　二○·一○　二○·四八　漲○·三八四十種債劵　　九三·一一　九三·一七　漲○·○六十一種物品　　六二·○九　六二·七二　漲○·六三金融外匯仍然硬化金價續跌二元半　　——半天形勢徘徊於五十元關口——金市人心雖尚穏定、然近日銀行方面盛傳將合作壓低匯市、冀中外匯價軋近、防止現銀流出之訊、匯市異常鬆濫、金市有套頭關係、賣户較殷、昨市續跌、晨初以海外銀市英美俱平、倫敦生金縮半便士、匯兌略長、美棉漲十四磅音、美麥升六二五、股票亦漲二元有零、物品毛盤開出平穏、但金業預備交易開後即跌、良以匯市鬆濫、銀行毫無買胃也、開後尚平、無如銀行胃口奇硬、賣方遂再奮勇、打破五十元大關、買方見低雖來活動、終因預悉匯豐掛牌突告放長、市况仍疲、但潛勢尚穏、人心亦平、此後塲内求過平衡、金價遂成盤旋之局、市况平庸者殊久、其後銀行賣胃略呆、華商仍有扒結、逐漸升至五十元外、中央亦有開現之傳、大户買氣頓蘇、内盤亦告微緊而漲、但銀行仍肯塞出、尚有回挫、盤旋之下、銀行胃口略告呆滯、又復漲高、但高後不乏脱手之流、午收爲狀殊屬平穏、平天間缺乏特殊消息、跌勢之成、依舊由於匯市之鬆濫、前途仍有盤旋、赤金價約照十二元、今將半天市况誌後、　　晨開爲五五○元二角、較前收下跌三元一角、物品開零六角、匯市晨開近期賣價英匯一先令四便士六八七五、美匯三十五元三一二五、永利兆豐昌雖進至一元二角、花旗塞十月份美金半元、以至五六二五、元一恒餘正昌大德成申康賣出、乃破五十元大關、退至四十八元二角、大發永慶餘進至五十元外、無如大英花旗塞十一月份美金六八七五、元昌氷鼎昌售條、又降爲八元半、福興永益成順巨乾昌祥雖進到九元外、終以預悉匯豐銀掛牌英升一二五、美長二五、内盤鬆濫、而跌至八元、大户如福泰亨丙興大發永大德成兆豐昌等俱售也、福興永乾昌祥兆豐昌大發永趁低來進、匯豐扒十月份美金五六二五、而升至九元三角、元一義豐永春源永尚有賣胃、然因大興永益成萬興恒興進條、乃盤旋於九元内外、極爲平穏、迨後中央有開現之説、大興永恒餘大德成元茂永元豐永惠祥鼎康物品俱進、十月份美金半元難結、而穿出五十元大關、升至五十一元半、福餘同泰昌源興脱乎、而告下游、銀行亦塞十月份美金半元、退至零三角、然因人心尚定、元茂永順茂趁低維持、尚堪拉上、入後十月份美金半元仍屬難結、元亨大德成乾昌祥餘慶永等紛紛買進、又漲到一元九角、趁高散户脱手、雖有買户、仍告回小、午收爲九五○元八角、物品拍同價、收市後初時似疲、但以福興永鼎昌俱有買胃、而告平穏、查半天間最高九五一元九角、最低九四八元、計三元九角起仆、結果較前收下挫二元半、　　結價因匯豐銀行美匯掛牌升二五、爲三十五元、合標金價九八八元强、照收盤價言、約撳三十八元弱、較之前收少撳四元有零、本月份登賬九五七元、九月份九五三元、十月份九五一元、上午補水九五七元、赤金價計九六二元二角、約照加十二元、津貨抵空、到頭仍略抵埠、塲内買户缺乏、大致天津貨進價照加十三元、但未成交、掉期形勢轉堅、大連帮萬興順利有所貼出、由鼎泰鼎昌福昌等貼進之、共約二百餘條、俱爲一元半、入後福昌愿意貼進、益成貼予恒餘一百二十六條、爲一元二角、最後約在一元光景、聞中央曾開現貨價約九五一元、仍爲多頭公司所經售之説、九月份條子、由福興永劃予福昌三百九十二條、價九五五元半、此外十月份亦互有劃賬、本月份及九月份條子已逐步减少、迄今天止本月份條子祇剩二十一條、計福昌居於買方、而大順居於賣方、　　場内交易平平、總計元茂永益成大興永大發永恒泰天豐恒永祥和鼎泰恒興源福餘兆豐昌惠祥福安順茂鼎康恒興等居於買方、義豐永元亨永豐春源永福泰亨乾昌祥同春餘慶永元一盈豐恒順利慶發永生大元昌永等居於賣方、鼎昌大德成恒餘申康鴻康永先出後進、永利兆豐昌先進後出、大連帮萬興共做二千六七百條、軋過略出、内有恒餘劃出八百四十條、順利共做八百有零、軋出一百餘條、廣帮生大出一百餘條、恒興進一百餘條、當天成交總數四萬四千五百零六條、　　九月份條子尚未掉妥者、計買方義豐永四百餘條、益餘三百零、福餘匯源大德成元茂永各二百以上、餘均零星、賣方計恒餘九百餘條、福昌盈豐恒各二百以上、乾昌祥元亨大豐恒各、百以上、總數二千零十六條、共計多頭十五家、空頭九家、　　十月期多空陣容、迄今天止、多頭計萬興七千四百餘條、順利六千一百餘條、元一五千二百有零、大德成三千九百餘、義豐永三千八百餘、元盛永一千五百餘、福昌恒餘各一千四百餘、大昌祥一千一百餘、元亨潤昌裕各一千有零、同豐恒順茂各八百餘、洽豐永七百餘、慶發永六百有零、大順五百餘、鴻興大豐恒鼎康各四百以上、空頭計乾昌祥六千四百餘條、正昌四千有零、福餘三千五百餘、益成一千九百餘、瑞興同春元茂永各一千四百以上、餘慶永元春大興永各一千二百餘、鼎昌申康各一千有零、源康祥八百餘、春源永元昌永大成同福各七百以上、恒興永德匯源祥豐森昌永元大永各六百以上益餘五百餘、震泰大發永成康各四百餘條、福安義生永亨宏利源興鴻康永恒泰惠祥各三百以上、籌碼總數四萬一千九百四十四條、共計多頭三十八家、空頭六十三家、銀行賣意不急滙市明暗俱鬆濫　　昨據外電、倫敦大條、以及美銀俱平、倫敦生金、縮半便士、英對美未動、美對英升三七五、英對法跌十三磅音、美對法長七五、匯市晨開與前收平價、近期賣價英匯一先令四便士六二五、美匯三十五元二五、開後即硬、良因近日銀行方面盛傳將壓低匯市、是以華商不肯輕易扒結、銀行賣意殊濃、開後即形鬆濫、匯豐銀行掛牌揭曉、英升一二五、美長二五、此際最硬、入後華商趁賤扒結、銀行亦有對做、過程乃平、迫後金市買户突殷、金價上升、華商買意遂切、而告微緊、但銀行不時供給、但賣意已較呆滯矣、九月分内外國債地方公債還本付息表（以有確實担保者爲限）名　　　　稱　利　率　發行額未償還額（二三·九·一·）九月份應付本息　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　總數　每百支元（一）日期　還本付息次總數期總數每百元支（二）　　（一）内國公債　　千　　　　元　千　　　　元　　　　元　　　　　元　　　　　　　　　元　　元整理六厘公債　年六厘　五四、三九二　三二、六三五　一○○支　　一　　——　——　　　　　三三　四八九、五三○　——奥賠二四庫劵　年六厘　　二、四○○　　一、七○四　　七一支　　二○　一五　二四、○○○　二一　　二五、五六○　一支續發二五庫劵　月五厘　四○、○○○　　二、 三十五元三一二五、較之前收計英平而美硬一二五華商奮扒美金一百餘萬元、而略塞遠期、又扒先令二三萬磅、銀行如花旗大通麥加利等賣意殊切、大英花旗又塞先令、今將半天成交錄後、　　英匯晨開近期賣價一先令四便士六二五、花旗塞十一月份下半月八一二五、三井扒十月份八一二五、華僑三井吃十二月份八一二五、大英售予洋行十月及十一月份七五、大英塞十月份下半月七五、朝鮮出匯豐九月份六八七五、花旗塞同月同價、午收賣價自一先令四便士六二五起至六八七五對搭七五止、進價加○六二五、　　美匯晨開近期賣價三十五元二五、花旗塞出十月份四三七五及半元、花旗麥加利三井大英塞十月份五六二五、華僑售予華比十一月份六八七五、匯豐納十月份五六二五、花旗上海大通塞十月份五六二五、大英花旗塞十一月份六八七五、大通華比麥加利塞十月份五六二五、三井吃十二月份七五、花旗華比塞十一月份六二五、三井朝鮮塞十二月份七五、大朝鮮塞十月份五六二五、大英浙江塞十月份半元、朝鮮扒十二月份六八七五、而塞十月份半元、朝鮮花旗塞十月份半元、華比三井扒十二月份七五、午收費價八九月份三十五元三一二五、十月份四三七五、十一月份五六二五、十二月份六八七五、買價照加○六二五、拆市加高劃頭亦增　　昨洋拆又見上挺、形勢步步遞昻、昨晨爲一角三分、午市同價、劃頭加水亦遞昻八分及一角、拆票交易早市轉賬三百三十餘萬、新交易三十餘萬、午市交易五十餘萬、小總會中交易二十餘萬、銀行收解、外商銀行收解票欵一百六十餘萬、各種貨匯什欵收解三百九十餘萬、外匯結欵一百七八十萬、出倉八十萬、華商銀行收解票欵二百四五十萬、各種貨匯什欵收解四百六七十萬、外結八十餘萬進倉五千萬、日商銀行收解票欵二百十餘萬、各種雜欵收解三百九十餘萬外結一百廿餘萬、進倉五十萬、錢莊洋公單收解三千三百餘萬、洋劃頭欵收解四百八十餘萬、各路匯欵八十餘萬、解現二三十萬、洋押欵交易八十餘萬、新做出一百六十餘萬、鈔票收回九十餘萬發出一百廿餘萬客路來源四十萬、去胃二十萬、又本市票據交換所二十二日交換總數、銀元八百三十七萬九千零九十三元九角二分、内計銀圓四百十萬零八千零十二元一角三分、匯劃銀圓四百二十七萬一千零八十一元七角九分、江廣兩角俱跌　　昨市江南小洋、微跌五角、爲八百三十四元、早午兩市輒同、收出交易早市四千角、午市二千角、廣東小洋、早市爲七百四十一元、午市跌一元、爲七百四十元、交易早市十一萬角、午市四萬角、銅元仍爲三百二十八千文、交易二萬六千八百九十六串、計代價洋八千二百元、紗花期紗後市賣出頓濃　　紗市續疲、跌風又起、以現紗銷路岑寂、午後商塲上忽生謡言、於是人心虚弱、賣風頓濃、但極大之抛空者未有、而錢莊帮之多頭、尚未吐放、市氣尚平、本月紗又降元半　　標紗前市開盤、美棉雖漲、而本月份紗以交貨充足、被其壓迫而落、遠月亦遭牽動、某廠亦套賣而錢莊帮之收貨問題、目前尚在計畫中、結果各月漲跌二·三·七角、午後聞現紗銷塲不暢、而市塲謡言甚盛、公債大落、開盤形勢嚴重、各月跌七·八角、但拍至二三盤賣風未見十分濃密、結果各月又跌八·九角至一元一二角、全日成交統計三萬九千四百五十包、查賣出信誠一千三百包恒大二千三百五十包、恒益一千三百五十包、惠康一千三百包、元一一千一百包、明德一千一百包、裕大六百包、泰昌九百五十包、買進通記一千零五十包、錦昌六百五十包、源大六百包、新昌七百包、元德一千七百包、長豐一千五百五十包、愼昌七百包、一日間最高低價及收盤列下、標　紗　最　高　價　最　低　價　收　盤　價　漲　　跌　存　賬　　數八月期　一八二·五　一八一·四　一八一·四跌一·五○　二五、四○○九月期　一八三·三　一八二·二　一八二·四　一·一○　五七、九五○十月期　一八四·九　一八三·九　一八四·○　○·七○　六六、八○○十一月期一八六·五　一八五·四　一八五·四　一·一○　五九、四五○十二月期一八七·五　一八六·五　一八六·七　○·八○　五一、七五○一月期　一八八·三　一八七·○　一八七·○　○·九○　四一、二五○總計　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　三○二、六○○紗銷祇六百餘包　　現紗銷路較清、查全日各帮買去統計六百五十包、行情平平、各帮買額如下、内地　八○　同行　一五　福建　一廣東　二○○天津　三五○標花略受紗跌影響　　棉市平、以美棉連日趨漲、賣風被其遏制、所以市情尚能穏定、惟後市紗市趨跌、隨之而下、但現棉開價尚堅、不過目前在新花登塲之際、賣方心神安定耳、鄭標平弱　　標棉前市開盤、隨外棉面堅、塲中新賣户不多、各月均漲五分至一角、午後開盤、以謡言紗市大落、各月隨之而跌一角至二角、全日成交統計六萬五千二百担、查賣出大孚一千七百担、惠康一千六百担、大昶一千六百担德記一千九百担、泰興一千六百担、長餘一千四百担、泰昌一千三百担、長和一千九百担、買進吉豐二千八百担、大豐一千五百担、源大二千九百担、愼裕一千担、新亨二千九百担、益豐一千六百担、穗隆二千三百担、恒昌一千二百担、同和一千六百担、一日間最高低價及收盤價列下、標　花　最　高　價　最　低　價　收　盤　價　漲　　跌　存　賬　　數八月期　三五·三○　三五·○五　三五·一○跌○·二○　八五、六○○十月期　三五·二五　三五·○五　三五·○五　○·一○　一七六、九○○十一月期三五·二五　三五·○五　三五·一○　○·○五　二五二、八○○十二月期三五·三五　三五·一五　三五·二○　○·一○　二二五、六○○一月期　三五·五五　三五·三五　三五·四○　————　一六○、七○○總　計　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　八六七、六○○廠需漸增　　現棉銷路仍平、新棉各廠進胃漸開、來源姚花到八百四十包、現花價如下、陜西花　　　四○·五○　申新廠進　　　六六○件　現貨送廠火機花　　　三八·七五　東棉行進　二、○○○包　抵押日廠姚花（市斤）三二·五○　廣帮進　　　　二二○包　現貨棧交陜西花　　　四二·五○　東棉廠進　　　二○○件　現貨送廠七月份本市外棉進日統計　　美棉　五六、八八一件印度棉　　五三、五六一件埃及棉　　　二、七六○件缅甸棉　　　一、四三九件非洲棉　　　　　七○○件美棉漲十五磅音　　昨美棉先因利物浦消息良好而堅、旋因南方套賣而疲、卒因空户抵補再昻、結果現貨漲十五磅音、期貨漲十二至十四磅音、英棉期貨漲一二點、印棉因利物浦消息良好而堅、結果平果爾漲一·七五羅比、奥姆辣漲○·五羅比、白羅溪漲○·七五羅比、原電錄左、（二十一日電）美棉　　　　比　上　日　合　國　幣　英棉　　比　上　日　合　國　幣十　　一三·五九漲一四　四二·○○　八　　六·九三漲二　四六·四○十二　一三·五五　一二　四二·四○　九　　六·九二　二　四六·五○一　　一三·六○　一二　四三·七○　十　　六·九○　二　四六·二○三　　一三·七一　一二　四三·一○　十一　六·八七　一　四六·○○五　　一五·八○　一二　四三·四○　十二　六·八七　一　四六·○○七　　一三·八八　一二　四三·七○現　　一三·五五　一三　四二·五○平果爾　一四六·七五漲一·七五　二二·五○奥姆辣　二○○·二五　○·五○　三○·○○白羅溪　二二二·二五　○·七五　五四·四○糧食旱秋粉麥俱回漲　　（粉市）粉市上午開盤後、各月份呈初平繼漲之象、以洋麥報價、芝加哥回好二三角左右坎拿大好四分至一角六分不等、當開價時、近期人心、仍見平定、惟遠期各月份、因業外投機多頭、仍以久旱無雨、各處災荒、勢所不免、故買氣又復重振、市面亦見高騰、是以二盤以下、即因此故、市况步見俏俐也、迨至下午開盤、近期因一無問津、且天津現粉報價、傳福新抛售、市價亦回鬆六角四分、开月底交割已近、買户有限、至遠期各月份、則内地帮及本埠外行買户、進胃甚健、故市面又步步良好、照目下情形而言、因秋收行將絶望、脚地似覺穏固耳、結果本月份較前日回漲三分半、九月份漲四分半、十月份漲五分、十一月漲四分二厘半、十二月份漲五分、一月份漲五分二厘半、　　（麥市）期麥市面、上午開盤後、各月份市面、均見高昻之象、以洋麥報價、芝加哥好二三角左右、坎拿大好四分至一角六分、故開價後、各月份市面、即較前日暗升數分、旋則抛出甚少、進户則頗健、市面即又步佳、本來業中人之態度、已極堅定、因産麗小麥有限、現麥局面、似難過落、人心一堅、市勢遂轉高較易也、迨至下午開盤、交易比較熱閙、本月份因交割之故、尚見平定、遠期則人心旣好、粉市又步振、故較上午又好幾分、結果本月份較漲八分、九月份好七分、十月份好六分、十一月份好八分、十二月份好一角、一月份好一角三分、現麥因各廠仍擯住不動、祗福新尚有應酬、開台兒莊山東徐州臨淮關麥三元九角八分、五河麥三元五角七分、江北清江麥三元九角四分、計共二萬餘包、新陳黄豆均堅穏　　昨日陳黄豆、雖愛前日餘威、但單靠囤户一路交易、人心不免虚弱、大勢見疲、交易減縮、計做開正陽關豆二車、穎州豆二車、南河次豆一百五十包、新豆因來源减少、去路尚接、且浦路一帶新豆恐有减收之謡、致貨户喊緊、行情續砌角譜、計成交早黄五百餘包、價爲三元八角二至八角、城門至開千外包、價目四元三角九至四元一角、江橋豆開三百包、價爲四元一角半及四元、去路聞均爲本街内地云、河米到頭漸稀　　各米俱見起色　　（滬西）昨各都來源續稀、仍惟十餘號、貨共二千餘户、買客時有問津、客帮包胃、青島帮續辦三四百包、故形勢殊見帶緊、市色有轉起之象、如各厚粳及晚稻行情結果、經售人一度喊聲、俱見增加一角、而杜洋尖陰變元等各花色、遂亦相繼挺秀尺許、新粳今已斷檔、聞須過旬日方可繼續蓮申云、　　（滬北）昨日河下各路來源十三四號、市上各貨去胃、白粳早稻早市平淡、午市稍轉活、羊杜尖略有白元薄稻平常、埠客尖東新粳交活、新客尖到少消平、市形白粳早稻轉緊數分、杜尖緊近角、埠客尖價加二角、其餘平定之勢、南北貨新桂圓不久有大批登塲　　新桂圓、惟廣東貨已稍有運到、首批較佳之貨、開二十九元、昨開轉跌三元、續有成交、趨勢平疲、其餘如同安安海泉州據函訊、不久亦可登塲、大約旬日内外、即有到申、届時市價必較陳貨爲低云、五金英鋼板廠銷獨健　　英鋼板市面、向賴客帮生意爲大宗廠家買賣、因大半向外洋直接訂定、所以在本埠購辦者爲數甚尠、近日來機器廠造船廠以及兵工廠等俱向市上購配、致岑寂市面、頓呈熱閙氣象、查二三日來被各廠購去之貨、爲數有二千二百餘擔、萎靡之市面、賴以站住、行情二厘半無大上落、此外半分估六元八角半、七厘半六元七角半、一分六元七角、一分半以上至四分每擔開六元五六角不一、但比之先前市價、各好一二角不等、惟觀最近外洋定價之高昻、及來貨之鮮少、申地頗有繼續開好之望、

申報本埠增刊談話關於青年職業問題  戊卯　　因爲北平的大學生組織了一個職業同盟會，于是青年職業問題，又成了社會人土一時注意的目標。有些人把這問題歸到青年自己身上，以爲青年的失業，是青年不能忍苦耐勞，不去求解决，有些人却以爲這是整個社會問題，青年自己是不負責任的對於這，我認爲有提出意見之必要。　　不把青年的失業，與全國經濟恐慌農村破産所産生的整個失業洪潮聨系起來看，自然是非常錯誤的見解。齊例來説，卽使全國大學畢業生，能够個個去拉黄包車，或者個個跑進工廠，也是徒然無益的事，因爲黄包車是有定數的，工廠畢竟只能容有限的人，進去一批，便要擠出一批，于是這一失業問題依然留下没有得到絲毫解决，這道理，是極其顯而易見的。　　然而，我們却也不能只看到一面，而忽視在現社會教育薰染下的知識青年。他們的墮落，他們的徒慕虚榮，形成他們徬徨歧路的主觀原因的存在。　　社會的條件，决定了青年的出路，青年的覺醒，却也足以把不利於己的環境轉移。如果我們把一切委諸社會，無異是教青年聽天由命，教青年靜待基督的恩典。這决不是解决問題的辦法。　　我所謂（覺醒），當然不是要青年去吹拍，要青年去屈就，這是無濟于事的，而是説有青年應該明白，自己與大衆並没有什麽不同，自己的出路，只有在大衆的同一行程上，才能尋到歸宿。　　不僅高官厚祿，是少數人的特權，在經濟破産，工商業凋零的情形下，裁員减薪，且是非常風行的事，這已不是學以致用的時代，青年所應該致力的，不是向上爬，而是前進，不是個人的出路，而是羣衆的出路，　　教育家們要青年埋頭讀書，埋頭練太極拳，以及不識不知地去埋頭苦幹，（這些恰是使青年墮落的原因）但青年是不需要這樣的；需要的是睜開眼看世界，理智地從實踐中去教育自己鍜鍊自己。假定自己的生活不與大衆的生活打成一片，失業的危機便永遠在你的周身，徒然請求救濟，是决無裨益的。車店之夜  懷瀛　　朝南的一連脊十大間草房，這五間西統屋就是車夫，旅客停宿的屋子，人們呌它（車房子）。南北窗下舖着兩面大炕，炕蓆破出大大小小的窟窿，像些紋絡。蓆面，一多半地上沾滿灰塵，一方面，因爲常久空着，没人睡，另外的原因在於車夫，旅客們爲了方便在炕上收拾東西或是趟着時不脱鞋，鞋底上是有灰土的。　　一盞大吊燈，吊在横樑上，燈罩灰土土土，發着不清亮的光輝。這不是進城賣糧的季節，院中車輛很少，屋裏旅客也不多，屋裏屋外都同樣的冷清。　　前後窗敞開着，夜的黑暗，一層層往屋裏侵蝕，大門外半里地以内的高山，看不見半點形影。　　依店主人説，没有閙事變以前，卽在夏季，儎車仍然很多的，所以生意還説得下去。事變後，道路上麻煩異常，車馬旅客因之减之。這是店主人的一種悲哀，悲哀他的生意和他的命運，後來他慨嘆着説：　　（這不是，諸位老客，今晚有你們七八位光臨，眞是我燒到高香，你們不知道十多天以來，没有一天上過五位客人的。）　　車夫也在述説他的苦衷，説他這生意簡直是有早上没後響的，碰到運氣好，多拉幾個錢，要走上惡運，就散臺了。他痛恨官家太不負責，不派兵剿滅沿路土匪，簡直不是保護人民的。　　旅客們的心思，才不一致呢，有的盼望早日回到家裏；有的憤恨路途多難，行路匪易，還要悲痛到時世的變遷；有的人又是天不怨地不怕的，遇到土匪，也没有什麽驚懼的，土匪不一定要人命使用。　　幾個人雖在談着閒話。可以説都是心不在焉，所以這麽説着，充其量不過是爲的來點綴這憂夜的沉悶罷了。　　約麽到半夜時候，屋裏幾個客人，除開我，都睡着了，有人還打着雷震般的鼾聲，一個番身，一句糢糊的囈語，似乎都含有無窮的意味。人家能睡這樣香甜的覺，我偏就失眠，幾聲隣家狗吠聲都要神精質的引得我的心房跳動不止　　吊燈還在點着，這是店家通夜不滅的長燈，不過燈芯由小夥計早擰小了，光亮就愈發顯得凄迷迷的。　　窗外馬圈，馬不住抬蹄抓着地，還打着噴嚔，嚼草嚼料聲也聽得清清楚楚的。馬糞味道，在發散着，在徑屋中散漫着。　　睡不着覺，頭裏面已然覺得昏昏的，惡濁空氣又刺激着我的鼻官，我實有離開這間（車房子）的必要，一狠心，他走到院心。　　在院中踱了幾躺步，遇到在糟頭守夜的更夫，他問我説：　　（老客，還没有睡？）　　（睡不着眠。）我答。隨又問他道，（你不想睡睡麽？）　　（哪敢睡，槽頭上有一匹馬，也要睜着兩眼守到天亮。）　　（這倒是一件艱苦吃力的工作。）　　（没有法子呀，苦也得忍受。）　　他説過這句難心話，也許由此句起他悲傷的往事，他憤憤的告訴我他兒子在一年前讓日本兵殘殺的事情，那眞是一點理由都没有，他問我有無評論道理的地方，是否有辦法可以伸伸寃。説到後來，嘴也許不給他運用了，只是不住地重念着下面的話：　　（這世界，没有講理的地方啊，没有講理的地方？没有啊。）　　他的手伸到眼睛上去揉，揉什麽呢？……失眠在熱帶的暴風雨之夕  漂流　　黯黑，暴風雨之夕。　　在牀上輾轉，不能寐。　　風在椰椰的梢上哭，是漂泊的浪子的哀號；雨擊在白鐵屋頂上，咚咚作響，是破碎的心底浪潮。　　狗在啼，（熱帶狗吠，煞像啼聲。）是幽靈哀號？雨點打着海水，轟轟作響，是流人的涙潮？　　望着灰黯的故國，想着鬢白的慈母，懷念着死亡的朋友，……這一切，讓失眠臨着這熱帶的暴風雨之夕！　　何處是熱情與愛？讓生命來掉在這蠻荒野島！何處有陽春烟景？讓青春給埋葬在這孤嶼荒郊！　　過去是，曾革了少年之命，曾戀了魔鬼之骨，曾蹂躪了貧苦者之魂，曾招來了死古人之魄，……　　於是，流亡在這蠻荒野島；於是，讓失眠臨着這熱帶的暴風雨之夕！　　故國，慈母，親愛的朋友，……　　一個小資産階級的煩惱！　　風在吼，南國之尖端！椰；海在呌，蘇門答臘底海濱。　　黯黑，失眠在這熱帶的暴風雨之夕！

回家  雋　　踏進家門，自然地感到一種很難得的温有的滋味。弟妹瞧見哥哥，娘瞧見兒子回來，笑盈盈的臉上充滿了説不盡的歡愉。一家之中馬上盈溢着久别重聚的天倫的樂趣，而那聖潔的人的眞情的流露的笑更使我這久已失去了童心的蒼凉的心被深深地感動過去。一些親人隣居亦都跑上家來，圍着我，張着熱摯的眼睛，和靄而又親暱的問這問那，一刹那間呌我完全陶醉在我的天眞無邪的境界中。　　這才眞是人生無窮的慰籍的樂園，家啊！　　來探視的人漸次各自散去這時太陽已射上屋脊尖頂。就近傍晚了。娘特地自家去上廚房燒飯，因爲第一天到家總得弄一頓特别的菜飯的。我獨自坐在庭前臨階上，最小的弟弟從學校裏回來，劈頭聽見娘説我回家，便在大井外邊一疊聲呌着：哥哥，一邊連跳帶跑的走進來，走到眼前，一點也不生疎的就抓着我的手腕。問着：有没帶什麽玩具給他。　　又一度嘗着人生眞切的暖意回家呵。　　這幾年老遠的離開家，在異地裏過流浪日子，已使我具有一個年輕的身而又年老的鬱悴的心。對於家的懷念早隨着時間緩緩地淡漠下去。　　如今又重新嚼味着家的温意，反而微微感到有幾分黯然的樣子。家呵。　　晚上，剛用過夜飯，爹從外面來了。就上明亮的燈光下，在廳堂上，一家人。繞在一塊談聚。不久二弟三弟都在打呵欠，爹呌娘先帶他們去睏覺再出來。娘隨便跟兩個弟弟上房子裏去了。　　留下爹和我，他坐在對面的坑塌上，半躺着身子，嘴裏咬着一支雪茄。一面用着他那依然嚮亮的嗓音。説着這幾年來家中的變化，親戚們的變化。説到去年生意失敗的時候，聲音猛的沉滯下來，而且每個音符裏都帶着一些微烟的傷感。説後，輕輕地嘆息了一口氣。又嘘了一口烟。　　聽了爹的話，聽了爹從來不曾有過嘆息的嘆息。除了接着他的嘆息在咽喉輕嚥了一口冷氣，在心裏邊無名地罩上了一層沉重的鉛塊之外。再也想不出什麽話來安慰他年老的心。以及用什麽方法處置自己凌亂的心。　　來了幾分鐘的沉默，在沉默的中間，我準着燈光射到的那面，靜靜瞧着半閉了眼睛躺着的爹。人是顯得異樣的蒼老了，頭髮已一根根在變白。雖然精神還是如從前矍鑠，可是我知道他的心靈是一天天的枯寂的，爲了這長長的日子紛繁的人事的推折，家的太重的荷負再加上事業不順意的劇烈的打擊，這此，全是呌一個上了年紀的爹感到世故的幻變的滄桑，而使思想過分的黯淡了。　　家呵！一下兒就變成這樣。回到家來，没得到别的，祇招來了更多的悲戚哀感。在我憂愁的心幕上又壓上一大塊憂愁的暗雲。　　眞没勇氣再在繁盛過的而今漸趨破落的家住着。過了幾天，只好忍着最大的痛苦，拭着無形的眼涙，離了家，背了最親密的人，重踏上流浪者征途，和一顆受創後的破碎的心一同地。雪齋雜語  雪爾　　入秋以來，正午依是不能跑出門去，（這是指我自己，馬路跑着趕着的不是人嗎？）憑天地良心，晚上倒底凉爽了。　　昨天友人送來一人副月餅，在陰歷七月中旬就吃到這種物品不可説不時髦了。晚餐後，我坐在窗前像煞有介事的吃起月餅來，因爲晚飯故意少吃了一碗的緣故，月餅的味道特别甜美。我想這好方法應該告諸國人，不然顯得我太吝嗇了，乃伸低吮筆預備寫了一篇（ＸＸ月餅）或（月餅ＸＸ）的文章。繼而想起一則笑話：一個鄉下人進城去辦貨，肚子餓了買兩個饅頭來充飢，吃完了還是餓，他再買兩個，……如是買了五次，才塞飽了他的肚子。他那時候也像我一般頓悟了什麽似的説：（早買了這兩個饅首（第五次的兩個）不是可以省許多錢嗎？）其實這笑話不見得十分可笑，然旣曰笑話，則我的（ＸＸ月餅），或（月餅ＸＸ）恐將來亦有被選笑話大觀的危機，迷巧一陣秋風吹窗口吹進來，把我寫文章的勇氣吹冷了，還是獨享我的月餅罷。　　一盒月餅共計四只，有蓮蓉，荳沙，百菓，腿肉，因爲味道不同，我想各個都嘗一點，不料吃開了胃，一上手（沙了蟹），肚子塡得結結實，比多吃一碗飯的時候還要飽。我想月餅也吃得飽肚子，這似乎又是應該説一説的，今年荒災奇重，大家吃了月餅，那些積囤米糧的朋友也該倒灶！於是再握起筆，但是今天眞怪，剛想下筆又想起一則故事：某國年歲大荒，各府各縣上奏聖上，王曰：（卽没有飯吃，何不食肉麽？）月餅雖不是肉麽，我也不是聖上，但是這年頭兒作事難就難在這點，若果這今事（與故事對）宣傳起來，不免有復辟思想，吃月餅而丢腦袋，患不着也，還是不寫爲妙。鄭逆手書宣言  金波　　八月十七日大阪朝日新聞載有影印鄭逆孝胥手書執政卽位宣言一幅，閲後不勝憤懣，以利祿薰心，不惜出賣國土之老賊，而敢妄言道德仁愛，爰將該宣言錄下，并仿其文以譏其事。　　人類必重道德，然有種族之見，則抑人揚已而道德薄矣，人類必重仁愛，然有國際之爭，則損人利己而仁愛薄矣，今立吾國以道德仁愛爲主，除去種族之見，國際之爭，王道樂土，當可見諸實事，凡我國人望共勉之。　　人類必重高官，然有名譽之見，則人得我失，而高官去矣，人類必重厚爵，然有人格之爭，則人有我無而厚爵去矣，今立吾志以高官厚爵爲主，除去名譽之見，人格之爭，榮華富貴，當可見諸實事，凡我國人望共勉之。這不是愛的  仃　　願意嗎》露珊！我陪你回去？　　不，我不需要。　　那末……一個子走路不是怪寂寞嗎？　　慣了，我常常那樣。　　　唷！一個女人夜裏走路不怕麽？　　怕什麽？　　鬼？流氓？醉漢？瘋子？白相人？你都不怕嗎？　　怕什麽！難道他們會把我吃掉麽？　　固然不會，可是，………　　怎樣？　　你不怕他們胡調嗎？　　胡調是不會駭怕的，于我也没有什麽損失。　　那末，你是説，高興他們胡調的，歡喜他們戲戲謔的：是不是露珊？　　瞎説！誰對你説（高興）？（喜歡）？　　喲咦……這不是明明白白告訴我嗎？　　什麽明明白白？　　你説：這于你没有什麽損失。那不是够了嗎？　　你眞是神經過敏！一個女人在夜裏走路一定會受人胡調嗎？就是縱使受了胡調，這有什麽大驚小怪呢？其實，就是受了胡調也没有損失的。損失了什麽？你説，你解釋給我聽聽……Ｃ先生。　　你的人格！　　啊？我的人格！我的人格就因爲他們偶然的胡調而受了損害嗎？瞎説！　　露珊！一個有人格的女子是不會受人嘲弄的，懂嗎？我愛你，所以，我要求你要尊重自己的人格。　　你愛我？Ｃ先生你愛我那點？你愛我的人格嗎？人格一斤值得多少錢？我是會有人格的人嗎？像我那樣的一種女子，爲了生活鐵索所鞭韃，弄至體無完膚，還説什麽人格不人格？　　露珊！我是愛你的。　　你愛我什麽？你你愛我的人格？笑話！你在欺騙我，你在玩弄我，踐踏我，想在我的身上，找尋一些剌激，快活，排洩排洩你的獸慾！　　胡説八道！我眞心愛你，反而你來駡我，露珊！你是懷了什麽一種心事？告訴我！難道我爲你受的犧牲還算不大嗎？我耗費自己的金錢，消磨我的光陰，荒棄我的事務，毁壞我的名譽，我的犧牲是多麽大啊！爲着你，露珊！我寗願犠牲自己，我愛你。　　這犧牲未免太大了。還是爲着你自是己罷！先生。　　Ｃ可我愛你。　　這不是愛的！　　那麽告訴我……這是什麽呢？　　這是毫無價值的浪費！　　那麽説，我們之間永遠没有結合的希望了。　　我們不會結合，我們没有愛情。我是爲着生活，把自己一生都糟塌了。而你，一般到這兒來的男子們，爲的也是找尋你們的快樂而已，用你們多餘的金錢和時間消耗在我們身上…………　　唉！這不是愛的，這是慾，這是萬惡金錢所玩的把戲。　　Ｃ君於是深深的嘆了口氣，一種抑鬱和悲感的情緒，突然在他的心裏擾亂起來。　　露珊的臉色，這時也蒼白的，眼睛是那麽惺忪和疲憊。她彷彿害了一塲瘧病似的，蹣跚地從那整整一夜没有歇息的舞塲出來。　　Ｃ伴着她傍邊，一面走，一面向她那麽説。　　成事　本刊二十日所載漫圖（禁止招貼），據讀者韓尚義君來函，曾登載去年三月份良友七十五期云，自應照章取消酬資，此啟　增刊編輯室無福享受  鎮球小説五家鎭上一件大事（三）  張一蘋　　每個人會意地點着頭，嘆服族長的有主見，富公公彷彿等候着這一句命令似的，從天藍夏布的窄袖管裏授出兩册褪了色的布面租簿。他謹愼地送到伍老太爺面前，端正地攤在柴檀几上，許多小組的頭顱都集中地圍上來向那租簿投着不同的目光。但是伍老太爺没有動手，誰都不敢先出頭的，　　（就這兩本嗎？）伍老爺注視了（民國十一年吉立，積德堂）伍字樣的封面動手翻起來。　　（是的，我們分家的時候就是這兩本。）　　富生站在他舅父張得福的背後，目光從前個子的肩頭射出來，他心中記熟着舅父告訴他的話。他已是二十五歲的男子了，在他十五歲的時候，他的叔父過世，膝下没有一個兒女，他是富公公的長子，就嗣出在他叔父名下。他親生的母親死得很早，富公公的塡房那時也生了五歲同三歲的兩個小兄弟。　　鄉村裏的俗語（討了晚（慢）娘連爺晚（慢））一個十五歲的孩子，他已知道得許多，並且鄰居間的閑言閑語他聽在小耳朶裏，他覺得父親待他是没有他兩小兄弟般的愛好。嗣出在叔父名下之後，就同父親隔居開來，父子間的感情慢慢地分離，這一次析産的發生，遠因就種在這裏了。　　因爲嬸母李氏自己旣不生兒子，嗣立富生，她也没有什麽成見。况且是一個女流之輩，對於一切田地上的往還都須要富公公經手，就把租簿交了出來託大伯代爲掌管，自己落得吃一口現成茶飯。　　在富公公呢，這也是義不容辭的。弟媳年輕寡居，兒子還没有掌握財權能力的年齡。　　富生新婚後的幾天，一個晚上，長工阿土到二房宅内説是老爺請少爺過去。自從十年來富生歸了嬸娘，父子之間更是隔膜，這一件醖釀着的析産問題誰都預料着富生討親後一定要發生的。嬸母起初是毫無成見，但是早夕有一個别人家的兒子來承歡膝下，自己年紀也漸漸地衰老，她爲身後算計，對於立嗣來的兒子同時特别愛憐起來。就以富生今年的討親來説罷，外面的事情自然有富公公出頭的，説起來總是他的大兒子討親。不過辦喜事，裏面的一切鎖零雜散，反不容易籌劃，况且男人家甚至不憧得的。富公公族人，親戚，鄉隣旣多，辦事自然更要煩雜。隔一層肚皮底富公公的塡房，她穿着整齊－紅裙禮服，戴了滿頭花，領着她自己的兩個兒子，祗向自家面上的親戚談長道短。

1934.08.23

Large-Scale Military Exercise 1

Japanese Troops Transported to Yuguan for Concentration; Many Civilian Houses Temporarily Occupied; Aircraft and Tanks Ready to Move Out; Warships Anchored in Qinhuangdao and Tanggu Waters

(Tianjin) Japanese troops stationed in Tangshan, Changli, Funing, and Beiping are scheduled to conduct combat and encampment exercises at the Sipingtai area of Yuguan for a week starting the 25th. Five aircraft will be dispatched from Jinzhou to participate in this exercise, and personnel from the puppet Manchukuo military and political departments will be invited to observe. Three hundred Japanese troops stationed in Tangshan, led by Battalion Commander Asami, took a special train on the Beining Railway on the 22nd and departed for Shanhaiguan. Japanese troops from Luanxian, Changli, and Funing will depart on the 23rd. One hundred and eighty Japanese troops stationed in Beiping were transported through Tianjin this morning at 5:00 AM to Shanhaiguan to join the large-scale exercise on the 25th. These troops are carrying four cannons, twenty-four machine guns, and military supplies in three freight cars. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Tianjin) For the convenience of the exercise, the Japanese troops in Yuguan have notified the Shanhaiguan Public Security Bureau to cut off traffic from the South and West Gates to the Japanese barracks south of the railway during the exercise. All vehicles, horses, and pedestrians are prohibited from passing. Starting from the 20th, the Public Security Bureau has dispatched police to begin evicting street vendors outside the South and West Gates. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Tianjin) One Japanese cruiser and three torpedo boats arrived in Qinhuangdao from the Tsushima Strait on the morning of the 20th and are anchored in the harbor. Two British warships and one Italian and one French warship are already stationed in the port and have not left for a week. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Tianjin) Starting today, Japanese troops in Tianjin have begun street fighting exercises in the concessions on Akashi Street, Fushimi Street, Matsugishi Street, Suma Street, piling up sandbags and setting up electric fences. They are preparing to begin the exercises after officers from the Third Fleet arrive in Tianjin at noon on the 22nd to observe. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Tianjin) Senior Staff Officer Oohashi of the Tianjin Japanese Army Headquarters has been transferred to serve at the Army University Research Institute and took an early ship back to Japan. Chief of Staff Kikuchi Mongokyu will meet with Commander Imamura of the Japanese Third Fleet on the 24th before returning to Japan. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Tianjin) After the cessation of the Yuguan Japanese army exercise, it was decided to hold a joint naval, land, and air exercise between Qinhuangdao and Yuguan, as well as outside Dagukou, on the 25th of this month. Various fleets have already been anchored in the waters off Qinhuangdao and outside Dagukou. Aircraft and tanks are also ready to move out. It is said that some civilian houses in Yuguan have been temporarily occupied, and small vendors outside the West City have been evicted. Japanese troops stationed in various locations will be transported starting from the 22nd. (Central News Agency Telegram, 22nd)

Japanese Aircraft Arrive at Malanyu 2

Unloading Large Quantities of Munitions

(Tianjin) Three aircraft flew in from the Northeast to Malanyu on the 21st, fully loaded with munitions, and stopped at the airport below Tashan to unload them. Japanese troops stationed in the town purchased over five hundred watermelons, which were carried back to outside the pass by the same aircraft to be distributed to the Kwantung Army and the puppet Puyi. (Central News Agency Telegram, 22nd)

(Beiping) Regarding the handover of the Eastern Tombs issue in Malanyu, Yin Rugeng will meet with Shibayama again today to negotiate. The Kwantung Army side has dispatched multiple representatives, but our side has not yet finalized the assignment. One company of security guards dispatched by our side to take over the Eastern Tombs has already arrived in Shimen Town and Malanyu. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

Drug Trafficking Organization Smashed in Qian’an 3

Japanese Side Plans to Protest 4

(Tianjin) The War Zone Security Team smashed a drug trafficking organization in Qian’an and arrested Japanese ronin Okamoto and Korean ronin Lee Chang-hwan. The Tianjin Japanese Consulate General is quite dissatisfied with this matter, claiming that our side abused Japanese and Korean personnel during the operation. On the 21st, two consulate staff members were dispatched to Qian’an to investigate, preparing to protest against us. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Beiping) He Huang, the chief of the Zunhua Public Security Bureau, has dispatched personnel to escort the drug-selling Korean Lee Chang-hwan to Beiping today, and immediately sent him to the Japanese Gendarmerie Police Station for punishment. The criminal confessed at the Jimi District Public Office that he was entrusted by the Japanese, Okamoto, to sell drugs in Zunhua and Jixian, and also confessed to firing a gun at the police and resisting arrest. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

Strictly Suppressing Narcotics 5

(Beiping) Strictly suppressing narcotics in the war zone, the Jimi District has already implemented it. The Luanyu District, due to its complex situation, finds suppression difficult. Tao Shangming will go to Tianjin in the next few days to discuss with Yu, and visit the Tianjin garrison commander and consul general. After the matter is completed, he will return to Tangshan and Yuguan to discuss with Asami of the Japanese garrison. Zhao Lei, Liu Zuozhou, Zhou Yuying, and Bao Xizhe are responsible for the security in the Luanyu District, and the provincial government will dispatch personnel to give instructions. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

Yuan Liang Hosts Banquet for Imamura Yesterday 6

(Beiping) Yuan Liang hosted a banquet at the city government this morning to welcome Imamura, commander of the Japanese Third Overseas Fleet in China, inviting Japanese Acting Chargé d'Affaires Wakasugi and others to accompany him. Yin Rugeng, Tao Shanggou, and others were in attendance. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

Shocking Drug Problem in Tangshan 7

(Tianjin) Japanese and Korean ronin have established twenty-six drug trafficking organizations in Tangshan, with over two hundred and thirty opium dens and morphine shops, harming countless Chinese people. Many families of small and medium-sized businesses have been reduced to beggars, and four or five people die in the streets every day. According to an investigation by the Public Security Bureau, more than eight hundred people died from narcotics from May to August 15th. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Tianjin) According to investigations, there are a total of two hundred and seventy-three foreign firms established by Japanese and Korean people in Tangshan. In recent months, due to strict inspections by the authorities, narcotics sales have been sluggish. Coupled with the market downturn, over twenty firms have closed down, and the rest are barely surviving. It is reported that six to seven months in Tangshan, more than eight hundred people died due to drugs, which is horrifying. - The Gubeikou Sub-Customs Office Established

Tax Collection Begins Immediately 8

Puppet Police at the North Gate Operate as Usual

(Beiping) The Gubeikou telephone and the Gubeikou Sub-Customs Office were officially established at 9:00 AM on the 22nd, without holding a ceremony. First, the Blue Sky with a White Sun flag was raised, followed by hanging the wooden plaque of the Gubeikou Sub-Customs Office of the Tianjin Customs District on the Great Wall. Then, they immediately started working, inspecting and levying taxes on goods entering from Huaikou. Representatives from various Chinese and Japanese organizations and gentry in the local area all went to offer congratulations, and Peng Danian, the director of the Sub-Customs Office, prepared tea and refreshments for the guests. It has been raining in Gubeikou since the 21st, and the 22nd did not clear up, resulting in very few imported goods. (22nd)

(Beiping) The puppet police of Gubeikou have been building new houses outside the pass, at Erdaoqiao, since this spring, and it is expected that construction will be completed soon. Currently, the puppet police at the North Gate of Gubeikou are performing their duties as usual, and the puppet police in the headquarters dormitory at the South Gate also have no plans to move. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Beiping) The telephone of Gubeikou and the Tianjin Customs Gubeikou Branch held an opening ceremony at nine o'clock on the morning of the twenty-second. Branch Chief Peng Danian took office at the same time, and representatives from various institutions and local gentry participated. Tax collection began on the same day. (Central News Agency Telegram, 22nd)

Approved by the Central Political Council

Zhejiang Provincial Bonds of 20 Million Yuan 9

Mainly Used for Disaster Relief

Approved for Issuance Before the Legislative Yuan Recesses

(Nanjing) The Central Political Council held its 422nd meeting on the morning of the 22nd, chaired by Wang Zhaoming, and resolved the following important cases: (1) The Nationality Law Convention and the Statelessness Protocol and the Statelessness Special Protocol were submitted to the Legislative Yuan for review. (2) The Executive Yuan's letter submitting the Merchant Debt Liquidation Ordinance was approved for record. (3) The Executive Yuan's request to temporarily allow the Xinjiang Provincial Government to establish an administrative office in Hami District was approved for record. (4) The Zhejiang Provincial Government was approved to issue Zhejiang Local Public Bonds for the Republic of China Year 23 (1934) for 20 million yuan. (Central News Agency Telegram, 21st)

(Nanjing) The Central Political Council resolved on the 2nd to approve Zhejiang Province's issuance of 20 million yuan of Zhejiang local public bonds for the Republic of China Year 23. According to a certain Central authority speaking to a Central News Agency reporter after the meeting, the main reason for the Zhejiang local public bonds is for disaster relief. The regulations and other items are currently under review. Due to the urgent need for disaster relief in the province, and the fact that raising funds will take considerable time, and the Legislative Yuan is currently in recess, it is feared that if the Legislative Yuan's procedures are completed, the disaster will worsen and it will be difficult to provide timely assistance. Therefore, today's political meeting specially approved its prior issuance. (Electric Report of the Fly Center on the 22nd)

Reconstruction and Rural Committee

(Nanjing) The Reconstruction and Rural Committee of the Executive Yuan has formulated a research outline and hired experts to conduct research. The outline includes three items: 1. Research on agricultural financial systems in various countries, (1) study the historical background of various countries and the development process of agricultural finance, (2) examine the organizational system, sources of funds, and current status of business expenses, (2) synthesize the evolution of various national systems and observe their trends. 2. The needs of our country's rural areas, the habit of emphasizing the infusion of capital, paying attention to the needs of rural areas in various places, the habit of emphasizing the infusion of capital, and its stagnation. 3. Based on the research results, formulate a plan for an agricultural financial system suitable for national conditions. Now, first translate Agricultural Financial System Theory, Agricultural Warehouse Theory, and Japanese Agricultural Financial System Theory, three books, as the basis for research. (Electric Report of the 22nd of the Month)

Wei Lihuang Orders Troops

To Advance to Gu Ping to Suppress Remaining Bandits 15

Bandit Luo Tuo Flees to Lianjiang

We Are Already Prepared to Intercept

(Fuzhou) The deployment of bandit suppression forces in Fujian Province is thorough both in the front and the rear, and a large-scale effort is about to be made to eradicate banditry, which is expected to be quelled. As for the bandits who fled from northwest of Luoyuan, because our troops were tightly encircled and their retreat was cut off, they dispersed and hid in Gutian, Shanyang, Hetang, Niutoutang, and other places, and in the Tianhu Road area of Pingnan, robbing and searching for food. Wei Lihuang has ordered various bandit suppression troops to advance to Gu Ping in different directions to join forces in suppression. It is also reported that the remnants of Luo Binghui's bandit troops have suffered heavy losses. Recently, they planned to flee to Lianjiang and join forces with bandit Wei Geng. Our army is already prepared to intercept them at a certain strategic location. (Central News Agency Telegram, 22nd)

(Guangzhou) Fujian merchants here received news from foreigners today that the bandit communists would attack Pucheng, looting fifteen villages and destroying eight thousand houses. The situation on the border between Hunan and Guangdong has stabilized. After defeating the bandits, the Hunan army has recovered Gui Dong. It is rumored that the battle lasted for fifty hours. (Reuters Telegram, 22nd)

(Fuzhou) The authorities ordered the air force on the 21st to continue flying over Ningluo and other places to reconnoiter and bomb the remaining reds, and to cover our army in its search and suppression. It is reported that the county towns of Ningde, Fu'an, Xiapu, and Fuding are all pacified. More than one hundred bandits in the eastern district of Xiapu were causing disturbances. After several bombs were dropped, the Xiancun area of Huotong in the northwest of Ningde was hit. The scattered bandits are showing signs of retreating. Our army is dispatching troops to block them. Wei Geng's bandit troops in Lianjiang will have our dispatched assisting troops arrive today to advance on the suppression. A considerable amount of force has also been deployed on the Gutian line to prevent them from causing disturbances. The electrical telegram indicates that the bandits on Jifeng Mountain in Huangli have retreated to Guikou. The bandits in Guixi have retreated through Luokeng and other places, showing signs of returning to Qingliu. The Datian bandits have retreated to Reshuikou. The bandits who were originally in Hongtian Ruozhu are still hiding. There are no traces of bandits from Gongchuan to Shangkou. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

Continuous Overcast and Rainy Weather in Beiping 18

Yellow River Breach

Floodwaters Reach Fan County Territory 19

Local Militia and Police Mount Dikes to Defend

Han Fuqu Inspects Huixian

(Jinan) According to a report from the River Bureau, the floodwaters from the breach have passed Puxian and reached the Daokou area of Fan County, more than thirty li from the county town, about one chi deep and seventeen or eight zhang wide, flowing at five li per hour. Bureau Chief Zhang Lianjia reported to the provincial government and telegraphed the county chiefs of Fan County, Shouzhang, Yanggu, and Dong'a to strictly prevent flooding in their respective sections. Today, he will return from Luokou to inspect the upstream area again. General observations indicate that the floodwaters from the breach will pass Fan County and Shouzhang and still enter the Zheng River through Taochengpu. The Shaanxi Hydrological Station telegraphed that the water level this afternoon was 292.48 meters, 1.6 chi lower than yesterday. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Jinan) Han Fuqu arrived in Fan County at 6:00 PM. He is scheduled to inspect Shouzhang on the 23rd before returning east and arriving in Ji'nan on the 24th. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Jinan) Tonight, the floodwaters reached Zhulou in Fan County, a little over eight li from Jucheng. The front of the flood was clear water, about one chi high, followed by yellow water, about two chi high. The Fan County militia and police mounted the dikes to defend all night. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Jinan) This morning, Han Fuqu went to Chaocheng from Yanggu to give a talk. A package of opium was found in the briefcase of Jin Ruheng, the accountant of the county government, and he was fined twenty yuan per liang. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Tianjin) Ma Xingang, the county chief of Puyang County in southern Hebei, telegraphed that after the Yellow River breach, two hundred bandits were found in the Xiaozhuang Gaocun area of Heze. On the 19th, the county chief supervised the local militia to pursue and suppress them. The Heze County police joined in the attack, and they were defeated. The remaining bandits fled towards Puyang. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Tianjin) The Hebei People's Office telegraphed on the 23rd that the three counties of Changyuan, Dongguang, and Puyang in southern Hebei must strictly guard against bandits after the Yellow River breach and step up their suppression. In addition, Zhang Yinglin, the county chief of Puyang, ordered the civilians to rush to block the Li Guozhuang water risk on the south bank of the Yellow River and provide disaster relief in coordination with Wang Zilin, a committee member sent by the province. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Tianjin) The floodwaters from the Yellow River breach are still flooding the Yian Town area of Huaxian County. Although the villagers built small embankments, they cannot prevent the flooding. More than 290 villages between Changyuan and Huaxian have more than 10,000 victims, all living exposed on the dikes. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Kaifeng) On the 22nd, the Yellow River iron bridge rose seven Chinese inches. The provincial party headquarters, considering the breach at the old mouth of Changyuan and the disaster in more than two hundred villages in Huaxian, telegraphed the central government and requested the Executive Yuan to quickly block the breach and provide disaster relief. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Beiping) Lin Chengxiu, the Director of the Hebei Construction Department, went to Changyuan to investigate the situation of the Yellow River breach. He arrived at Xinxiang on the 22nd and arrived at Daokou Town on the 21st, and immediately went to Changyuan to investigate everything, supervising Changyuan County Chief Bu Hengxu to rush to block the breach on the Jiugulu. Lin telegraphed a report, waiting for the water to recede and return north, and requested that relief agencies quickly devise a way to provide relief. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

Purchasing Rice from Hunan to Operate Stabilization Sales

Jiang replied that in addition to the Hubei provincial government raising one million on its own, the central government decided to establish a grain transport bureau to handle stabilization sales. As for the provincial government's one million relief fund, 60% has already been raised, and 100,000 will be allocated from provincial bonds. The annual production of public property will also be sold to coordinate disaster relief. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

Ancient Temple in Nangong County

Fifth Generation Sutras Discovered in Cave 32

(Tianjin) The ancient temple in Banbi Tang Village, Nangong County, Hebei Province, is abandoned and uninhabited. Recently, tourists discovered a dark hole in the hall. There were brick walls like a Buddhist hall with Buddha statues and incense tables, and there were ancient scriptures in wooden boxes, numbering five hundred. People went to inspect and determined that they were left over from the Liang Dynasty of the Five Dynasties, and their value is very high. Recently, the Xinke County Government has heard of this and sent personnel to take custody, which will be turned over to the Provincial Government for preservation. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

Current Commentary

>　　現存額不敷戰時兩年之用　　阿拉斯加錫鑛擬着手開採 33

The current amount is insufficient for two years of wartime use. Alaskan tin mines are planned to be developed.

（華盛頓）依六月十五日衆院外次委員會今日着手調查美國錫的供給問題、據國備院人員聲稱、世界錫產、美國銷费過半、但操緃錫業者爲國際恊定、而美國不與焉、外國出產家乃據此協定、於過去兩年中提高錫價一倍云、國務院維志氏稱、美國現不產錫、如遇戰爭、則美國所可有之錫、不敷兩年之用云、委員長麥克瑞诺稱、美國現擬發逹錫業、阿拉斯加現亦擬開採錫礦云、（二十一日路透電）

(Washington) According to a statement by personnel from the National Preparedness Board, the House Foreign Affairs Subcommittee began investigating the issue of tin supply in the United States today, June 15. The statement claims that the United States consumes more than half of the world's tin production. However, tin operations are controlled by an international agreement in which the United States does not participate. Foreign producers have reportedly raised tin prices by 100% in the past two years based on this agreement. Mr. Weiji of the State Department stated that the United States currently does not produce tin, and in the event of war, the tin available to the United States would not be sufficient for two years. Chairman McCraino stated that the United States is planning to develop the tin industry, and Alaska is also planning to develop tin mines. (Reuter, 21st)

榖繭價賤日本農村困苦　　農林省亟籌救濟

Cheap cocoon prices cause hardship in Japanese farming villages. The Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry is urgently planning relief measures.

▲東京通訊本年物價大賤、前所罕遇、農民所產之榖繭、得價甚微、致農压大困、而呈不安之象、故政府來年必須依更大之規模、繼續其救濟工作、並當實施蘇息農民之永遠計畫、農林省現議請大藏省在來年預算案内撥欵二千七百萬元、以充救濟經費、晨林省亦擬撥一千三百五十萬元、實行舠定繭價之永遠計畫、永野爲日本産繭要邑、該地議會曾開緊急會議、通過議案、宣布政府今應許該邑農民停止還債三年、此爲絶對必要之舉云、其債欵共約七千三百萬元、此爲欠各銀行者、若連其他債欵計之、當有四萬萬元之多、每人應負一千三百元、今售出之繭、當不足償付債欵之利息、故當急予救濟也、衆意永野議會之行動、或將使其他産繭區迅速發生反響、（十七日路透社）

▲Tokyo Correspondent: This year's commodity prices are extremely low, which is rare. The price of cocoons produced by farmers is very low, causing great hardship and unrest among farmers. Therefore, the government must continue its relief work on a larger scale next year and implement a permanent plan to relieve farmers. The Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry is currently discussing requesting the Ministry of Finance to allocate 27 million yuan in next year's budget to provide relief funds. The Morning Forest Province also plans to allocate 13.5 million yuan to implement a permanent plan to determine cocoon prices. Nagano is an important cocoon-producing area in Japan. The local council held an emergency meeting and passed a resolution announcing that the government should allow farmers in the city to suspend debt repayment for three years, which is absolutely necessary. The total amount of debt is about 73 million yuan, which is owed to various banks. If other debts are included, it will amount to more than 400 million yuan. Each person should bear 1,300 yuan. The cocoons sold now are not enough to pay the interest on the debt, so relief must be given urgently. It is generally believed that the actions of the Nagano Council may cause a rapid reaction in other cocoon-producing areas. (Reuters, 17th)

意奧兩揆谈話結果維持奧獨立完整　　兩國政治經濟　　王室稪辟認爲尙非其時　　奧地利共和國改稱聨邦　　奧揆離意赴法之尼斯小作勾留

The outcome of the talks between the Prime Ministers of Italy and Austria is to maintain Austria's independence and integrity. Political and economic relations between the two countries. The royal family believes that the restoration is not yet the time. The Republic of Austria is renamed the Federal State. The Austrian Prime Minister leaves Italy for a short stay in Nice, France.

佛洛倫斯今日奧總理許希尼格博士與意相墨案里尼在十六世紀馬里魯斯别墅會談時、復聲明奧國獨立之不可侵犯忣兩國政府予以维持之决心、談話後發表公報稱、两總揆已在政治經濟文化範圍內、建定有實效的共同目的與方法、對奧國安全與其内部売全自主之维持、亦復妥協、兩總揆並同認三月十七日羅馬議定書之有益、及决議繼續進行在經濟範圍内發展合作之政策、又意奧間之文化關係、亦將從事鞏固之、增多互換大學敎授與學生及旅行家之人數、爲期應施辦法之一公報中又言及終將商勸捷克加入羅馬協約、且聲明兩總揆並未談及哈浦斯堡王室復辟事、謂此非目前之急務、供给奧國借欵事亦未談及云、墨索里尼在談話後、卽逕返山間、觀意陸軍之大操、奧總理返奧前、擬至法國尼斯一行、據未徴實之謡言、渠或將與法政府之代表一晤云、（二十一日路透電）AA佛洛倫斯奧國總理許士尼格今日接見記者、除對於墨索里尼崇揚備至、及感謝意國所予奧國之援助外、並稱、奧國並未變更其對德之根本態度云、（二十二日國民電）AA羅馬奧國總理許希尼格在佛羅倫斯與首相墨索里尼會晤竣事、於今午由慹諾亞乘船赴法國尼斯城、將在該處斯電）

Florence - Today, during talks between Austrian Chancellor Dr. H希尼格 and Italian Prime Minister墨案里尼 at the 16th-century馬里魯斯 villa, they reiterated the inviolability of Austria's independence and the determination of both governments to maintain it. A communique issued after the talks stated that the two Prime Ministers have established effective common goals and methods in the political, economic, and cultural spheres and have reached a compromise on maintaining Austria's security and its internal and completely autonomous. The two Prime Ministers also agreed on the benefits of the March 17 Rome Protocol and resolved to continue the policy of developing cooperation in the economic sphere. Furthermore, cultural relations between Italy and Austria will also be strengthened, and one of the measures to be implemented is to increase the number of exchanges of university professors, students, and travelers. The communique also mentioned that the Czech Republic will eventually be persuaded to join the Rome Agreement and stated that the two Prime Ministers did not discuss the restoration of the Habsburg royal family, saying that this is not an urgent matter at present, and the issue of providing loans to Austria was also not discussed. After the talks, Mussolini returned directly to the mountains to observe the Italian army's grand maneuvers. Before returning to Austria, the Austrian Prime Minister plans to travel to Nice, France. According to unverified rumors, he may meet with representatives of the French government. (Reuter, 21st) AA Florence - Today, Austrian Chancellor许士尼格 met with reporters and, in addition to praising Mussolini and thanking Italy for its assistance to Austria, stated that Austria has not changed its fundamental attitude towards Germany. (National Telegraph, 22nd) AA Rome - Austrian Chancellor許希尼格 has concluded his meeting with Prime Minister Mussolini in Florence and will travel by boat from Genoa to Nice, France, this afternoon, where he will (this is from the telegraph).

（倫敦）英國報紙研究昨夜意相墨索里尼與奧總理許希尼格會議後發表之公報、認意奧兩國已進一步合作對付德國、每日民聲報認意國已以奧爲其保護國云、此外以特萊斯脱爲根據地、而開辦奧國航業、亦爲最受注意之事、此間以為奧國航業將完全受意人之操縱云、（二十二日國民電）

(London) British newspapers are studying the communique issued after last night's meeting between Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and Austrian Chancellor 许希尼格, believing that Italy and Austria have further cooperated to deal with Germany. The Daily Herald believes that Italy has made Austria its protectorate. In addition, the establishment of Austrian shipping based in Trieste is also a matter of great concern. It is believed here that Austrian shipping will be completely controlled by the Italians. (National Telegraph, 22nd)

不啻對德警告奧復辟談不到

No less than a warning to Germany, there is no question of Austrian restoration.

羅馬（泰回萊報）評讑意相墨索里尼與奧總理許希尼格在佛羅倫斯之會唔、謂意奧兩國總揆之晤覿、不僅有裨於意奧兩國之邦交、且兩國與歐洲其他各國諒解之精神與合作之志願、亦於此獲一明證云、（批哥羅報）則謂就政府發表之公報、兩國總揆會晤所談論者、不僅係奧國之獨立、且涉及奧國領土之完整與政洽之自主、今如有人造作是非、謀爲不軌、施其詐欺、逞其陰謀、則聆此警告以後、當必收藏不義之武器而銷聲匿跡矣、奧國不能受人保護、不論完全保護或巧立名目、均非奧國所甘受若輩旣不得逞、若復假借恢復哈布斯堡皇室之名義、以施其詭謀、則當對之日、奧地利共和國與其政府、均不願聞此類問題也云云、（廿二日哈瓦斯電）

Rome (泰回萊報) commented on the meeting between Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and Austrian Chancellor许希尼格 in Florence, saying that the meeting between the two Prime Ministers is not only beneficial to the relations between Italy and Austria, but also a clear proof of the spirit of understanding and the desire for cooperation between the two countries and other European countries. (批哥羅報) said that according to the communique issued by the government, the meeting between the two Prime Ministers discussed not only the independence of Austria but also the integrity of Austrian territory and political autonomy. Now, if someone fabricates rumors, plots misconduct, deceives, or schemes, after hearing this warning, they must hide their ill-gotten weapons and disappear. Austria cannot be protected by others, whether complete protection or under any guise, which Austria is not willing to accept. If those people cannot succeed, and they borrow the name of restoring the Habsburg royal family to carry out their schemes, then on the day of facing them, the Republic of Austria and its government do not want to hear such questions. (Havas, 22nd)

兩揆初握手

The two Prime Ministers shake hands for the first time.

佛洛倫斯意首相墨索里尼與奧總理許希尼格今日在佛洛倫斯附近墨氏之馬林尼别墅晤談一小時这久、此爲奧總理人意後第一日之談話、當奧總理車抵佛洛倫䔮時、墨氏會親至車站迎迓、奧總理當卽在車站廣塲上兩國國樂洋洋聲中檢閲榮譽警衛隊、事後二人卽驅車至斯堪迭西之安丁諾里别墅、該處卽意政府爲奧總理特備之行轅、午刻墨氏復在其馬林尼别墅設午宴欵待、陪宴者有奧國駐羅馬代辦、意國外交次長蘇维區、泛繫黨總幹事斯逹雷斯、情報司司長齊亞諾、及意大利駐奧公使等多人、午餐後意相與奧總理卽入别室密谈、事後墨氏卽遄返意北、檢閲该處之野戰演習、聞奧總理已由意政府邀請參閲該項操演、（廿一日國民電）

Florence - Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and Austrian Chancellor 许希尼格 met for an hour at Mussolini's馬林尼 villa near Florence today. This was the first day of talks after the Austrian Prime Minister took office. When the Austrian Prime Minister's car arrived in Florence, Mussolini personally went to the station to greet him. The Austrian Prime Minister immediately inspected the honor guard on the station square amidst the sounds of the national anthems of the two countries. Afterwards, the two drove to the安丁諾里 villa in Scandicci, which was specially prepared by the Italian government as the Austrian Prime Minister's residence. At noon, Mussolini hosted a luncheon at his馬林尼 villa. Those accompanying the luncheon included the Austrian charge d'affaires in Rome, Italian Deputy Foreign Minister Su维區, Pan-League Secretary-General 斯逹雷斯, Director of Intelligence齊亞諾, and the Italian Minister to Austria, among others. After lunch, the Italian Prime Minister and the Austrian Chancellor entered a separate room for private talks. Afterwards, Mussolini quickly returned to northern Italy to inspect the field exercises there. It is reported that the Austrian Chancellor has been invited by the Italian government to attend the exercises. (National Telegraph, 21st)

德奧間關係

Relations between Germany and Austria.

维也納此次意奧兩政府首領晤談之集中黠、厥爲德奧間之關係、此係奧都政界方面之見解、彼等復稱、無論在意方或奧方、均覺中歐政治情形之改善、首在德奧關係之發展、奧國之政府機關國家郵報今日謂、德奧在多瑙河區域問題中、以經濟分配之方法、積極合作、其於將來密切關係之需要、實不亞於德國在四國公約中關係歐洲全部合作之重要云、（廿一日國民電）

Vienna - The focus of the meeting between the leaders of the Italian and Austrian governments this time is the relationship between Germany and Austria. This is the view of Austrian political circles. They also stated that, whether in Italy or Austria, they both feel that the improvement of the political situation in Central Europe lies first in the development of German-Austrian relations. The Austrian government agency, the National Post, said today that Germany and Austria are actively cooperating in the issue of the Danube region through economic distribution, and its need for close relations in the future is no less important than Germany's relationship with the entire European cooperation in the Four-Power Pact. (National Telegraph, 21st)

（柏林）今農各報對於意奧兩首揆之會晤評論甚少、惟柏林交易所日報爲例外、该報社論謂駐奧公使巴本晋謁米格拉斯總统時、米氏答詞會谓（渠主張設法排除奧德間之一切經濟障碍、）該報以爲維也纳政府對於（奧德和解問題）擬先由弳濟方成着手、但經濟問題之研究頗費時日、且經濟問題重受政治關係之影響、以是兩者不能分别研究、交易所日報復陳述、其素來主張之理讑、謂德國派遣巴本爲駐奧公使、並採取若干毫不含糊之辦法、可見德國絶不欲奧國獨立發生問題、德國所希望者、僅奧國獨立能爲各國所一致承認耳、交易所日報以爲就此層言、奧德之和解絶無任何障碍、惟許希尼格内閣須眞能平定奧國、然後奧德經濟問題始能有效談判耳、庶德奧兩國有密切與親善合作之可能、柏林日報反駁聨邦郵報之論調、謂如要求德國發表宣言、保障奧國之獨立、則合作結果卽不能逹到云云、（二十二日哈瓦斯電）

(Berlin) Today, the newspapers have little comment on the meeting between the two Prime Ministers of Italy and Austria, with the exception of the Berlin Stock Exchange Daily. The newspaper's editorial stated that when Ambassador巴本 to Austria visited President 米格拉斯,米氏 said in his reply that (he advocated finding ways to eliminate all economic obstacles between Austria and Germany.) The newspaper believes that the Vienna government intends to start with the economic aspect of the (Austrian-German reconciliation issue), but the study of economic issues takes a lot of time, and economic issues are heavily influenced by political relations, so the two cannot be studied separately. The Stock Exchange Daily reiterated its long-standing argument, saying that Germany's dispatch of巴本 as its ambassador to Austria and the adoption of some unambiguous measures show that Germany absolutely does not want the issue of Austrian independence to arise. What Germany hopes is only that Austrian independence can be unanimously recognized by all countries. The Stock Exchange Daily believes that, from this point of view, there are absolutely no obstacles to Austrian-German reconciliation, but the 许希尼格 cabinet must truly stabilize Austria before Austrian-German economic issues can be effectively negotiated, so that there is a possibility of close and friendly cooperation between Germany and Austria. The Berlin Daily refutes the arguments of the Federal Post, saying that if Germany is required to issue a declaration guaranteeing Austria's independence, the result of cooperation cannot be achieved. (Havas, 22nd)

奧政策不變

Austria's policy remains unchanged.

佛洛淪斯奧總理許希尼格博士今日語客、謂奧國一旦有完全之自由、有作内政外交之决議、及其政策爲各國所承認時、則與德國恢復平日之關係、自無阻力、奧國基本政策以多瑙河流域約及千年之德人使命爲根據者、今仍未變動、此次渠之訪晤意相墨案里尼、蓋出於深感上月意國助奧平亂之訧衷、渠與意相之談話、乃在特殊性質下進行、而有助於　兩國間之關係、並爲已故總理杜爾夫斯博士政策之一種直接賡續云、（廿一日路透電）

Florence - Austrian Chancellor Dr. 许希尼格 said to a guest today that once Austria has complete freedom to make decisions on domestic and foreign affairs, and its policies are recognized by all countries, there will be no obstacles to restoring normal relations with Germany. Austria's basic policy, which is based on the Danube River Basin Agreement and the thousand-year mission of the Germans, has not changed. His visit to Italian Prime Minister Mussolini this time was out of a deep sense of gratitude for Italy's assistance in suppressing the rebellion in Austria last month. His talks with the Italian Prime Minister were conducted under special circumstances and were helpful to the relationship between the two countries and were a direct continuation of the policies of the late Prime Minister Dr.杜爾夫斯. (Reuter, 21st)

法對意懐疑

France is suspicious of Italy.

（巴黎）奧總理許希尼格與意相墨案里尼之會晤日期、與陶爾斐斯之被刺僅隔數星期、報界認爲意義重大、小巴黎人報謂佛羅福斯發表之公報、與本年二月英法意三國保證奧國獨立之宣言完全相合、晨報謂現在不可知之點、爲意大利究將在如何範圍之内考慮保障奧國之獨立、但意大利政府似相信左右若干情形之下、惟使用實力始能眞正有效、巴黎迴聲謂意大利是否不思由英法籨訂一種公約、以保障奧國之獨立、並以保障之任務委許意大利、此層殊爲疑問、（埃克西有報＋謂昨日意奧兩首揆進行之談話、本年秋間法外長巴爾都拜訪羅馬時、必將繼續行之、（斐卡羅報）謂奧大利問題、僅有一種解决方法、卽就政治與經濟問題、使奧匈意三國與小恊商各國互相接近、簽訂一種多瑙河條約以多瑙河政策維持多瑙河和平、藉以保障奧國獨立是也、意大利外交蘇维區對晨報駐佛羅惀斯記者云、（此次兩首揆會晤、既未談任何新條約、亦未提及任何新協定、哈布斯堡皇室復辟問題不獨未嘗討論、抑且未嘗提及、吾人與奧國政府均認此黠非現在所當討論之問題）云、（廿二日哈瓦斯電）

(Paris) The date of the meeting between Austrian Chancellor许希尼格 and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini is only a few weeks after the assassination of陶爾斐斯, and the press believes that it is of great significance. The Little Parisian reported that the communique issued by佛羅福斯 is completely in line with the declaration guaranteeing Austria's independence by the three countries of Britain, France, and Italy in February of this year. The Morning Post said that the unknown point now is the extent to which Italy will consider guaranteeing Austria's independence, but the Italian government seems to believe that, under certain circumstances, only the use of force can be truly effective. The Paris Echo said that it is doubtful whether Italy is considering concluding a convention with Britain and France to guarantee Austria's independence and entrusting Italy with the task of guaranteeing it. (埃克西有報+ said that the talks between the two Prime Ministers of Italy and Austria yesterday will definitely continue when French Foreign Minister 巴爾都 visits Rome in the autumn of this year. (斐卡羅報) said that there is only one solution to the Austrian problem, that is, to make Austria, Hungary, and Italy and the countries of the Little Entente close to each other on political and economic issues and sign a Danube River Treaty to maintain peace in the Danube River with the Danube River policy in order to guarantee Austria's independence. Italian diplomat蘇维區 told a reporter from the Morning Post in Florence that (this meeting between the two Prime Ministers did not discuss any new treaties or mention any new agreements. The issue of the restoration of the Habsburg royal family was not only not discussed but also not mentioned. We and the Austrian government both believe that this issue is not something that should be discussed now). (Havas, 22nd)

Budapest - The government is paying close attention to the meeting between the two Prime Ministers of Italy and Austria in Florence, but the attitude of the press is extremely reserved. The Roman government seems quite surprised by Hungary's attitude. (Havas, 21st)

意防軍撤退

Italian Defense Forces withdraw.

（柏林）七月廿五日奧國政變發生之後、意大利軍隊會開赴意奧邊境以備萬一、嗣見奧國大局漸定乃逐漸撤退、此間攻撃報頃刊登意大利軍隊由佛利由地方撤退時之相片題有（無功而返、）略謂、（意大利軍隊七萬五）千人全副武裝、興高采烈、開抵勃倫納山隘、當時奥國副總理史泰亨堡親王見時局不安岌岌自危、意大利軍隊固準備開進奥境、以維持秩序者、實則無須出此今果無用武之地廢然而返矣、意軍此行長途跋涉、惟若於患足病者而已、死傷則一無所有、吾人稱之爲（無功績之遊行）可也）云云、（二十日一日、哈瓦斯電）

(Berlin) After the coup in Austria on July 25, Italian troops went to the Italian-Austrian border in case of emergency. Seeing that the overall situation in Austria was gradually stabilized, they gradually withdrew. The attack newspaper here recently published a photo of the Italian army withdrawing from佛利, with the title (Returning without merit), briefly saying: (The Italian army of 75,000) thousand people, fully armed, arrived at the勃倫納 Pass in high spirits. At that time, Prince史泰亨堡, the Deputy Prime Minister of Austria, saw that the situation was unstable and precarious. The Italian army was indeed preparing to enter Austria to maintain order, but in fact, there was no need to do so, and they returned in vain. The Italian army's long journey was only for those suffering from foot disease. There were no deaths or injuries. We can call it (a march without merit). (Havas, 21st)

德國社黨又一陰謀敗露　　在米美爾組成兩種政治團體　　圖煽起暴動使之脱離立陶宛

Another conspiracy by the German Social Democratic Party is exposed. Two political groups were formed in 米美爾. Plotting to incite riots to separate it from Lithuania.

立陶宛京城德國國社黨曾在米美爾地方組成兩種政治團體、一爲社會主義勞工恊會、一爲社會主義人民恊會、目的在於鼓動暴動、使米美爾地方脱離立陶宛、當道已對該兩政治團體提起訴訟、關於訴訟進行情形、司法部長曾發表宣言加以説明、半官式立陶宛日報評論此項宣言、謂（米美爾地方陰謀、在籌備期内卽被破獲、此則與維也納叛變（指七月二十五日之叛變）不同之點也、陰謀領袖現在獄候審、一俟訴訟不久結束以後、國社黨陰謀詳情卽可公諸世人、德國各報一見陰謀敗露、卽開始恫嚇、須知司法手續將照常進行、固非威脅所得阻止者也、立陶宛已將國社黨面具揭破、現非進行到底不可、立國始終嚴格立於本身權利範圍以内、今後亦將如此、但决不容外國于涉其内政也）云云、（廿一日哈瓦斯電）

Lithuania's capital - The German National Socialist Party had formed two political groups in 米美爾, one was the Socialist Labor Association, and the other was the Socialist People's Association. The purpose was to incite riots to separate 米美爾 from Lithuania. The authorities have filed lawsuits against the two political groups. The Minister of Justice has issued a statement explaining the progress of the lawsuit. The semi-official Lithuanian Daily commented on the declaration, saying (The conspiracy in 米美爾 was discovered during the planning stage, which is different from the Vienna rebellion (referring to the rebellion on July 25). The leaders of the conspiracy are now in prison awaiting trial. Once the lawsuit is concluded soon, the details of the National Socialist Party's conspiracy can be made public. As soon as the German newspapers saw that the conspiracy was exposed, they began to intimidate. It must be known that judicial procedures will proceed as usual, and threats cannot stop it. Lithuania has unmasked the National Socialist Party and must now proceed to the end. The country has always strictly stood within the scope of its own rights and will continue to do so in the future, but it will never allow foreign countries to interfere in its internal affairs). (Havas, 21st)

希特勒施展鐵腕征服反對份子　　柏林四郊大捕勞工遇抵抗　　天方敎徒公然向希黨挑戰

Hitler exerts an iron fist to conquer opposition elements. Large-scale arrest of workers in the suburbs of Berlin meets with resistance. Muslims openly challenge the Nazi Party.

（柏林）星期日之人民投票、中有百分之十反對希特莂、柏林國社黨對於此等反對份子、已開始採取所謂（感化手段、）據昨晚柏林四郊報告、已有勞工多人被捕、惟此種感化手段之進行、並不如國社黨領袖預料之平安無事、於逮捕此等工人之時、向日横行無忌之褐衫黨員、竟遭彼等抵抗、此猶爲國社黨秉政以來一年中之第一次也、不少工人皆絶對拒絶随往衝鋒隊分部、以致引起數處暴動、工人雖赤手空拳、猶盡力抵抗、終到地同往警署而不受褐衫黨員之拘捕、據國社黨分析此次投票、反對者四百萬票中、至少有二百萬票係天主敎區所投、尤以萊茵一带爲甚、故現已竭力設法使天主敎徒皆加入國社黨、其餘二百萬票大部分爲柏林漢堡·及其他大城市中所投、欲其服從國家社會主義殊非易易、天主敎機關報今日對於希特勒爲欲感化二百萬敎徒、已向之挑戰、该報重載希特勒之青年圑領袖霍伯於八月中所發議論、謂（我等青年應竭盡全力、以與基督敎作最後之奮鬥、德國應脱離敎會之束縛、因敎會係外人主持、使我等皆被猶太人所利用而已）云云、該報現在要求國社黨對於此種議論作一解釋、（廿一日國民電）

(Berlin) In Sunday's plebiscite, 10% opposed Hitler. The Berlin National Socialist Party has begun to adopt so-called (persuasion methods) for these opposition elements. According to reports from the suburbs of Berlin last night, many workers have been arrested. However, the implementation of this kind of persuasion method is not as peaceful as the National Socialist Party leaders expected. When arresting these workers, the Brownshirts, who used to run rampant, were resisted by them. This is still the first time in a year since the National Socialist Party came to power. Many workers absolutely refused to go to the Sturmabteilung branch, which caused riots in several places. Although the workers were unarmed, they tried their best to resist and finally went to the police station together without being arrested by the Brownshirts. According to the National Socialist Party's analysis of the voting, at least 2 million of the 4 million votes against it were cast in Catholic areas, especially in the Rhineland. Therefore, they are now trying to get Catholics to join the National Socialist Party. Most of the remaining 2 million votes were cast in Berlin, Hamburg, and other large cities, and it is not easy to make them obey National Socialism. Today, the Catholic press challenged Hitler for wanting to persuade 2 million believers. The newspaper reprinted the remarks made by Hitler's youth group leader霍伯 in August, saying (We young people should do our best to fight the final battle with Christianity. Germany should get rid of the shackles of the church, because the church is run by foreigners and makes us all be used by Jews). The newspaper is now asking the National Socialist Party to explain these remarks. (National Telegraph, 21st)

The Customs Administration Cables Jianghan Customs to Cease Collecting Consolidated Tax Cargo Bund Construction Fees. The Jianghan Customs has been ordered to cease collection. Refund of Taxes Collected Previously, According to Shen Shi News Agency, cargo that has completed consolidated tax payments should not be subjected to double taxation at any point. This has been repeatedly telegraphed and ordered by the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance. Recently, the Jianghan Customs in Hankou suddenly received an order to levy a Bund Construction Fee starting August 1st. This applied to all goods that had already paid the consolidated tax, such as cotton yarn, cement, and matches, which is clearly inconsistent with the order. Previously, the Chinese Merchants Yarn Mill Association and the Japanese Textile Industry Association jointly requested the Tax Administration to ask the Customs Administration to telegraph the Inspector General of Customs to order the Jianghan Customs to cease collection, in order to emphasize tax policy. Now, the Customs Administration has telegraphed to inform them to cease collection. A reporter from Shen Shi News Agency has specially investigated and recorded the original letters and telegrams below. Customs Administration Telegram. The Customs Administration Director Shen Shuyu telegraphed the Tax Administration: Tax Administration Director Wu Qiting, Brother, esteemed Sir, I have received telegrams from Qin and Zheng requesting the Jianghan Customs be ordered to cease collecting Bund Construction Fees, etc., on cotton yarn and other goods that have already paid the consolidated tax. I have ordered the Inspector General of Customs to order the Jianghan Customs to cease collecting the Bund Construction Fees levied with the consolidated tax, and to investigate and refund the relevant fees levied on consolidated tax goods after August 1st. I am sending this special telegram for your reference. Brother, Shen Shuyu, Official Seal. Letter to the Yarn Mill Association. After receiving the telegram, the Tax Administration sent Official Letter No. 1129 separately to the Japanese and Chinese Yarn Mill Associations, stating: "Respectfully, we received your letter stating that the Jianghan Customs has been collecting Bund Construction Fees on cotton yarn and textiles imported and exported in the Hankou area since August 1st, and requesting that we forward a request to stop this. After receiving your letter, this Administration has already telegraphed the Customs Administration to forward a request for a halt on this matter. Now, we have received a reply telegram from the Customs Administration, stating that the Inspector General of Customs has been ordered to order the Jianghan Customs to cease collecting Bund Construction Fees on goods that have already paid the consolidated tax, and to investigate and refund the Bund Construction Fees collected after August 1st. This letter is sent accordingly. To the Japanese Textile Industry Association in China, the Chinese Merchants Yarn Mill Association, August 20th." The Consulate in New Coven Reports That Overseas Chinese Are Unable to Donate. The Shanghai Charity Organizations Federation for the Relief of Northeastern Refugees received a reply from the Deputy Consulate in New Coven, USA, stating: "Respectfully replying, your letter has been received. The 32 donation booklets for the relief of Northeastern refugees previously sent by your association to our consulate were handled by the former Deputy Consul Mr. Li Zhaosong. There are not many overseas Chinese in our port, and most of them are engaged in the laundry industry, which is extremely difficult. Fundraisers from within the country are also arriving one after another, making them feel overwhelmed. We have heard that former Deputy Consul Li mentioned before returning to China last fall that the fundraising had no results. We are accordingly reporting the situation in a letter for your kind attention." Enthusiastic Registration of Dock Workers at the Dock Industry Affairs Office. Xin Xin News Agency reports that since the Municipal Dock Industry Affairs Office began handling registration, the work has been intense, and the registration staff in each district are particularly diligent. Recently, due to the relatively quiet business at the docks in the Nanshi District, the workers are scattered and constantly moving, which has slightly affected the registration progress. However, the dock workers in the Pudong District have repeatedly sent representatives to request that the registration of that district be done first. Therefore, the office has now complied with their request and transferred some of the Nanshi District registration staff to work in Pudong. At docks such as Taikoo, Huatong, Hongsheng, Longmao, Mitsui, Qichang, Huazhan, and Hanyeping, registration is actively underway and the results are very good. It is reported that the foremen and supervisors at each dock are also providing a lot of assistance to the office's registration efforts. Since the labor and management sides are not working against each other, the successful completion of this registration can be foreseen. As for the docks on Suzhou Creek, Longhua, Wusong, and in the Special District, the office is currently in contact with them separately and will begin registration soon. Anhui Jing County Natives Provide Disaster Relief for the Drought. Since the beginning of summer, Jing County in southern Anhui has not had rain for three months. The crops have withered and there will be no grain harvest. Various public organizations in the county have sent telegrams and letters to natives in various places, appealing for relief. The natives of Jing County in Shanghai, recognizing this situation, held a special meeting yesterday. Dozens of people including Hu Puan, Zhu Jingan, Wei Shoujing, Zhu Zunyi, Zhu Xiaoshan, Wei Shoushan, and Hu Huisheng attended. It was decided to organize the Shanghai Jing County Natives Temporary Drought Relief Committee to raise donations from natives in Shanghai to purchase large quantities of grain and transport it back for price stabilization. Zhu Douwen, Zhu Rushan, Zhu Jingan, and Wei Shoujing were appointed on the spot to be responsible for fundraising. The Director of the Shanghai Social Bureau, Wu Xingya, received instructions from the municipal government yesterday, stating approximately: "The Ministry of Interior's Note No. 161 concerning the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's presentation, based on a proposal from the Pawnshop Trade Association, requesting the Social Bureau to stipulate women's clothing styles, and that all men and women's clothing should use domestic silk, satin, gauze, Luo silk, homespun cloth, and summer cloth has been forwarded to the government to eliminate bizarre clothing styles. For clothing materials, it is also requested that domestic goods be adopted as much as possible throughout the country. The Executive Yuan has been instructed to have the Ministries of Interior and Industry jointly respond. In addition to separate letters, the original documents are enclosed and forwarded for investigation. This is approved. After investigation, promoting domestic goods and eliminating bizarre clothing styles have been previously circulated and forwarded by this Ministry for compliance. In November of the 21st year, Central Committee member Chen Zhaoying proposed strictly using domestic goods and eliminating bizarre clothing styles. The Executive Yuan ordered a joint resolution to be made by the Ministries of Military Affairs, Navy, Industry, Education, etc., and requested the circulation and forwarding of instructions for police agencies to actively implement them. The previous letter is approved. In addition to a reply and separate forwarding, the original presentation from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce is enclosed and forwarded for investigation and instructions to the relevant departments to actively dissuade and prohibit these practices. One original presentation is attached." This is approved. The original presentation is enclosed and sent to the relevant bureaus with instructions for the Social, Public Safety, and Education Bureaus to comply with the elimination and promotion efforts. This order is issued. After receiving the order, Director Wu and others, considering that the case involved promoting domestic goods and complying with the elimination of bizarre clothing styles, discussed methods for promoting domestic goods and eliminating bizarre clothing styles at the Social Bureau at 2:00 PM yesterday. In addition to Sun Yongyi from the Social Bureau, representatives from the Education Bureau and Jin Zhongjian from the Public Safety Bureau also attended. The Municipal Government Prohibits the Yinxiang Horseracing Competition. Selling Tickets and Horse Tickets is Not Allowed. The municipal government reported that the Yinxiang Racecourse recently purchased a large number of towed carriages and racehorses from abroad in the name of the International Horseracing Club and added various facilities inside the racecourse to hold regular night races and sell tickets and horse tickets in accordance with ordinary horseracing methods. The municipal government authorities considered that the International Horseracing Club had neither applied for registration nor followed horseracing procedures to report in advance. If it sells tickets without authorization, it will be in violation of the regulations. Therefore, yesterday, it ordered the Public Safety Bureau to strictly prohibit it. The Domestic Manufacturers Association Plans to Hold County-Level Touring Exhibitions. Filings Have Been Separately Submitted to the Jiangsu Provincial Government and Provincial Party Headquarters. The Shanghai Chinese Domestic Manufacturers Association believes that its participation in the Jiangsu Provincial National Exhibition has been highly effective. If the National Exhibition is extended to the entire province and country, its effect will be even more profound. In recent years, imports of foreign goods have increased without decreasing. Promoting domestic goods and expanding publicity are essential plans. The association recently plans to hold a touring exhibition of domestic goods in various counties throughout Jiangsu Province and has separately submitted filings to the Provincial Government and Provincial Party Headquarters, requesting filing. On the evening before last (the 21st), it held a banquet for various circles in the provincial capital at the Dahua Hotel in Zhenjiang. The details are recorded below. Filing to the Provincial Government. The Chinese Domestic Manufacturers Association sent filings to the Jiangsu Provincial Party Headquarters and Provincial Government yesterday, stating: "Filing is for the holding of a touring exhibition of domestic goods in various counties throughout Jiangsu Province. We request your approval for filing and kindly ask you to issue a notice to all counties to provide assistance to facilitate the progress and maintain domestic goods. It has been found that imports of foreign goods have exceeded hundreds of millions of dollars annually. The outflow of money has led to today's overall economic collapse. The central government has listed the domestic goods movement as one of the seven national salvation movements. Recently, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has also adopted the domestic goods movement into the New Life Movement and listed it as a top priority. The only way to stop the outflow is to resist the dumping of foreign goods. The only way to resist the dumping of foreign goods is to actively promote domestic goods and expand the domestic goods movement. The most effective method for the domestic goods movement is to hold domestic goods exhibitions. This association was invited by the Jiangsu Provincial National Goods Exhibition Preparatory Committee to lead member factories to the province to participate. Since its opening on August 1st, tens of thousands of people from the provincial capital have visited the exhibition every day. The voice of promoting domestic goods has resonated throughout the provincial capital. Although it may not be known to everyone, it has already had a considerable effect. In order to expand the domestic goods movement and enable people throughout the province to understand domestic goods, after the provincial national exhibition closes, we will carefully select domestic goods products and send them to various provinces and counties for large-scale touring exhibitions, in order to awaken the people throughout the province to a deep understanding of domestic goods. However, this matter is of great importance and requires the assistance of local governments to handle it, and to provide convenience will not be in vain. Therefore, we specially submit this filing to your department (government). We request that you issue a notice to all counties that when the subordinate association arrives to hold the domestic goods movement, they will assist in the handling to facilitate progress and maintain domestic goods. We are most eagerly awaiting your reply." Banquet for Various Circles. On the evening before last (the 21st), the Chinese Domestic Manufacturers Association held a banquet for various circles at the Dahua Hotel in Zhenjiang. Representatives from the Department of Civil Affairs Wang Ziqi, Xi Shaoting, Chen Boqin, representatives from the Provincial Party Headquarters Shi Shunyuan, Peng Chao, Pan Guojun, from the Provincial Government He Changcha, Chen Xun from the County Government, Liu Jinsheng from the Department of Finance, Zhou Xingfu from the Public Security Bureau, Wang Songquan from the Land Bureau, Huang Junbo from the Provincial Chamber of Commerce, Zhu Yunsheng from the Mass Education Center, Zhou Yuanbo from the County Party Headquarters, and more than 80 people from the Business Tax Bureau, Stamp Tax Bureau, Bank of Communications, and the press attended. Chen Binghui and Liu Zhongying, standing committee members of the association, and Ren Suizhi and Lin Letian, factory representatives, provided warm hospitality and various domestic goods manufacturers used a lottery method to distribute domestic goods gifts to help increase interest. " It is heard that Gao Jun has already accepted the request and is responsible for carrying it out. The Shanghai Telephone Bureau Announces to Users to Urge Payment of Machine Deposit Fees. All Supplementary Payments Must Be Made by the End of This Month. Otherwise, Lines Will Be Cut and Calls Will Be Suspended According to Regulations. Since the Shanghai Telephone Bureau implemented the conversion to automatic machines last year, traffic facilities in the Chinese area have gradually become perfect. Moreover, the cost of this automatic machine is high, and the annual rent and interest paid to the China Telephone Company are very high. In order to make the income and expenditure of the Telephone Bureau match, the Ministry of Communications specially instructed the Shanghai Telephone Bureau to clear up the machine deposit fee of five yuan paid by each user installed before May of the 22nd year, and uniformly changed it to ten yuan in national currency. Users have been notified in advance, but users feel that the economic burden has increased and it is really beyond their ability. The businesses and residents of the Zhabei District jointly requested the cancellation of this measure in order to maintain business difficulties, but the Shanghai Telephone Bureau is acting on the orders of the Ministry of Communications and is unable to accept users' requests. Moreover, it has been found that users throughout the city (those installed before May of the 22nd year) have been actively paying supplementary machine deposit fees. Therefore, this machine deposit fee will still be refunded in full when the user removes the phone in the future, and only a small number of people are opposed to paying. Therefore, the bureau specially issued a second reminder notice yesterday, limiting the supplementary payment to be made by the end of this month. If it is overdue, the lines will be cut according to regulations. The notice is recorded below: "Respectfully, it has been found that the amount of machine deposit fee paid by users of this bureau is inconsistent, and the Ministry of Communications has instructed that all users installed before May of the 22nd year be strictly cleared up and uniformly charged ten yuan in national currency. This bureau has already sent a letter urging payment. It has now been found that your account has not yet been paid, which not only hinders the bureau's sorting procedures but also fails to implement the uniform principle of the ministry, which is very inappropriate. Therefore, we are sending another letter limiting you to bring your old receipt and the amount of silver to be paid to the business section of this bureau by the end of this month to exchange receipts. If you delay again, this bureau will have to handle it according to the regulations. Please do not delay. Sincerely yours, Xu Xueyu, Director of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications." Special Investigation Record of Domestic Industry. Natural Economy and National Crisis. The more pressing the tighter, the decline of rural areas, the weakness of purchasing power, and the sluggishness of the business market all affect the manufacturing industry. The manufacturing industry is the essence of the country's salvation. In the thousands of threads of national salvation, the first priority is to use domestic goods and self-sufficiency. What is the current situation of various domestic industries recently? It should be woven in three dimensions and measured with numbers. Interview leaders of the industry on the ground. Although fragmentary, the general situation is seen. It is called a bird's-eye view, and perhaps there is something to it. (1) Canning Industry. Shanghai's canning industry has a history of 16 years, starting with the Huacheng Canning Factory in the 8th year of the Republic of China. Later, with the surge in demand from various places, the establishment of canning factories increased day by day. Up to now, there are as many as 27, but only seven have joined the trade association. Users of various industries need canned equipment, on the one hand, to maintain the cleanliness of the goods and are not easily damaged, and on the other hand, the beautiful decoration attracts consumers' love and storage concepts, and has advertising properties, so the use is becoming more and more extensive and the demand is increasing. It has occupied a considerable position in the domestic goods business. In particular, the Kangyuan Canning Factory has gradually progressed with a small capital to a share of 1 million yuan. It is rare to operate in a miserable way. I visited Mr. Xiang Kangyuan, the manager of this factory, and learned a little about the industry, and wrote to the Chinese people. Although there are many players in this industry, only seven have joined the trade association. The trade association was initiated by Mr. Xiang, the leader of the industry, three years ago. Unfortunately, many factories have not joined. The total sales of domestic goods each year is more than 2 million yuan. The Kangyuan Factory accounts for about three-quarters of it, which is 1.5 million yuan. Due to the popular sales of domestic goods, foreign goods have almost become extinct. The number is very small. Although the trade association has been established, competition between the same industry is inevitable. However, Kangyuan Factory is strong in capital, technology, and management, and always seeks rationalization. Everything pays attention to reality and recognizes the four words (genuine goods at a fair price). If you actively do it, you will not be affected by any competition and there is no need to compete with all walks of life. As for the sales of products, domestic canning technology has been improving day by day recently, so the popular sales of domestic goods have almost made foreign goods extinct, which is very gratifying. When asked about the difficulties in manufacturing and promotion, Mr. Xiang said that there are many difficulties. First, the donation tax is heavy, second, the transportation is inconvenient, third, the raw materials are lacking domestic production, and fourth, the social purchasing power is weak. The sales area is Hua, except for Shanghai. South, such as Guangdong and Hong Kong, Nanyang Singapore, North China such as Tianjin Yantai, and the Yangtze River Basin. Also, are there any failed factories in the same industry? The answer is not many. The reason for the failure is entirely due to the passive and suicidal meaningless competition. In the future, if the same industry can unite and compete on the quality and materials of the products, the future is very promising. Mr. Xiang said that in the development history of Kangyuan Factory, what is most needed is the iron sheet. There is no such product in China, so it is bound to rely on imported products. At present, the industry is working hard to plan in order to achieve the goal of self-manufacturing and avoid being monopolized by foreigners. Mr. Xiang's statement is very pertinent and said that the achievements of this factory are not something that personal knowledge can do. For example, building a house, from design to implementation to completion, how much is the work of the carpenter, how much is the work of the mason, how much is the work of the worker, and how much is the work of the engineer, which is not easy to analyze or calculate. The foundation of this factory is roughly available, and it is all the result of cooperation. The reporter still remembers that Mr. Chen Guangfu said that our country's factories can serve the society and solve various difficult problems for the employees. Mr. Xiang should be the first person. Mr. Wang Yunwu said that among our country's factories, the one that has both scientific management and worker welfare is Kangyuan as the first family. These two sentences are not exaggerations. Representatives of the Tobacco and Wine Industry Will Go to the City Chamber of Commerce Today to Petition. Reduce the License Tax.
