Chen and Zhang said that because the investigation procedures of each association have not been completed and there are many households in the tobacco exchange industry that have been heavily taxed, copying the list is time-consuming. It is scheduled to meet with Chairman Yu this afternoon to discuss everything. A Mad Dog Bites People in the French Concession and the Authorities Announce Precautionary Injections. The French Concession Board of Directors, due to the occurrence of multiple cases of mad dogs biting people in the concession, in order to avoid the spread of infection, announced to residents in the concession who have dogs yesterday: "Announcement: It has been found that there have been multiple cases of mad dogs biting people in this concession. Therefore, in order to avoid the spread of infection, this board has taken strict measures. All dog owners should strictly abide by Article 1 of the board's regulations for managing dogs on the road. If there are dogs without muzzles walking on the road, the police are entitled to arrest them and put them in the dog prison. This board hopes that residents in the concession who have dogs will inject their dogs to prevent rabies. Please be informed. Fules, General Manager." The Southeastern Transportation Exhibition Prepares to Print ("Southeastern Scenic Spots"). Shen Shi News Agency, this city news. The preparatory committee of the Southeastern Transportation Exhibition previously invited more than 100 famous celebrities and literary writers, Ye Yuhu, Wu Zhihui, Liu Yazi, Huang Renzhi, Yu Dafu, He Tianjian, Lang Jingshan, Zhao Shuyong, etc., to visit the scenic spots on the originally planned routes of the exhibition and solicited their respective strengths to write poems, travel notes, Western sketches, and photography works, etc., which have all been handed in one after another. Most of them are carefully crafted masterpieces with valuable value. In addition, youth literary works were solicited, divided into four categories: poetry, prose, Chinese painting, Western painting, and photography. The results are also very impressive. A public exhibition was held at the YMCA in Baixianqiao in this city, and viewers gathered and praised it. Wang Yingbin, director of the publicity group of the association, is using these valuable works to prepare and print a book ("Southeastern Scenic Spots") to expand publicity and leave a permanent memorial. However, because the content of the book is mostly pictures and photographs, high-quality paper must be used, and the printing must be exquisite in order to maintain the original appearance. The collection is already rich, and it cannot be contained without a huge volume, so the cost of the book is very expensive. At 6 yuan per book, printing 10,000 books requires more than 60,000 yuan, and the cost of entertaining more than 100 famous celebrities and literary writers, inviting them to visit all the scenic spots in the five southeastern provinces, soliciting youth literary works awards, and the cost of taking intaglio copper pictures are not included. Moreover, the purpose of the book is for publicity, commemoration, and tour guidance, so the price should not be too high. Therefore, it is necessary to rely on advertising revenue to supplement the funds. It has now been negotiated that the United Advertising Company in this city will be the advertising manager for this book, and Cheng Yuqing, a cadre of the association, has been transferred to Shanghai to work with the company to actively promote it. The association also believes that the importance of editing talents is essential, and fortunately it has obtained the consent of Zhao Junhao and Lang Jingshan to serve as text and art editors, respectively. Zhao Jun is the editor of Travel Magazine, and Lang Jun is also a famous artist in Shanghai and is familiar with the scenic spots in the southeast. The content of the book is a masterpiece by celebrities, and it has been compiled by experts. It is expected that when this book is published, it will be expensive like paper in Luoyang. The New Strategy of Expanding the Zhengda Bank. The Zhengda Bank on Jiangxi Road in this city has been open for many years, and it has long been known for its reputation in the financial industry and has gained a superior position. Therefore, in recent years, its business has become increasingly prosperous. The original address was narrow and could not meet the office needs. Therefore, it obtained the consent of all shareholders and decided to increase capital, hire experienced people, and expand the scope of business. It decided to build a magnificent new building at No. 25 Tianjin Road. After a long period of planning, it has now been completed. It is scheduled to move to the new address and officially open on the 24th of this month (that is, tomorrow). It is expected that there will be many congratulatory guests and merchants gathering, which will add to the grand occasion. A reporter from Xin Xin News Agency specially inquired about the issuance date with the bank yesterday, and it was said that the supplementary banknotes are scheduled to be issued starting September 1st, but the amount to be issued has not yet been determined. Fortunately, the owner's family had many people and quickly drew water to extinguish the fire, preventing a major fire. Only the bed curtains and bedding were burned, and the loss was minimal. However, two people, a man and a woman, were burned in the fire. They were later sent to Renji Guangren Hospital for treatment by street police. The man, Liu Jiansheng, 28 years old, injured his hands and feet. The woman, Chen Zhu, 45 years old, suffered severe burns to her chest and arms.

Page 13

Four Black-Clad Ghosts Drag a Shoemaker into the River

- A Ghost Story, Please Listen to it With a Grain of Salt -

The Shoemaker Sees a Ghost in Broad Daylight and Loses Control of Himself

The Black-Clad Ghosts Drag Him into the Water, Nearly Drowning Him.

Although today's science is advanced, no one can definitively say whether ghosts exist or not. Yesterday, at the Youche Wharf on the Huangpu River in the Nanshi District, a shoemaker was suddenly dragged into the river by four demons, nearly drowning him. This incident is quite strange and unpredictable. This newspaper has conducted an on-site investigation and found the incident to be true. Therefore, we are recording the details below for readers to study.

A Harmonious Couple.

Liu Baoxiang, a native of Gaoyou, Jiangsu, is 24 years old. He runs the Liu Changxing Shoe Shop at No. 134 Duojia Road in the Nanshi District, specializing in fitting shoe soles for nearby residents and boatmen. His monthly income is enough to make a living. Liu is usually very healthy and has no mental illnesses. His wife, Xi, is 21 years old. They have been married for four years, and their relationship is quite harmonious. Last summer, Xi gave birth to a son, but he died of illness soon after. Later, she was introduced to work as a wet nurse at the Zongji Charcoal Shop in Nanmatou, sending her monthly wages back to the shop to supplement the family income.

Demanding Overdue Wages.

A Shandong man named Dai Shunheng is a kiln cargo boatman. All of his new and old shoes are repaired by Liu Baoxiang, resulting in an accumulated debt of two yuan in labor costs, which has not yet been paid. Yesterday around noon, Liu, after lunch, learned that Dai Shunheng's kiln cargo boat was docked at the Youche Wharf on the Huangpu River. He took the time to go there, intending to demand the overdue payment. Unexpectedly, when he arrived at the Youche Wharf, Dai's boat had already sailed to another port, and he was unable to find him. He returned disappointedly.

Four Black-Clad Men.

Suddenly, as Liu passed the Shanghai Public Hospital at No. 53 Duojia Road, he heard someone shout behind him, "Shoemaker, slow down! Dai's boat is still on the riverbank, I can lead you there." Liu immediately stopped and turned around. He saw four men, all wearing black short shirts and pants, speaking with a northern accent. They were all about two chi (approximately two feet) tall and around 20 years old. Their faces were all black, resembling coal workers. The strangest thing was that the four men's faces, clothing, figures, etc., were exactly the same. At that time, the four men were waving and running towards him.

A Blurry Scene.

Seeing this, Liu was suspicious. However, because it was broad daylight and the sun was shining, he did not suspect ghosts. But after the four men waved to Liu, his mind was still clear, but everything he saw was very blurry. Even his body was out of his control. He turned around and followed the four men straight towards the riverbank. Liu saw the four men walk to the Youche Wharf and then jump onto the wooden rafts floating on the river, stepping on the rafts and moving forward. Liu followed them. When they reached the end of the wooden rafts, they still did not see Dai's boat.

Forcibly Dragged into the River.

Liu asked the four men where Dai's boat was docked. The four men replied in unison, "Dai's boat is docked at the outer anchorage. If you want to go, we have a boat that can take you there." After saying this, the four men jumped into the river one after another. At this point, Liu realized that the four men must be demons. As he was about to turn around and escape, the four men emerged from the water with ferocious faces and grabbed Liu's feet, dragging him into the river. At that moment, Liu was terrified and screamed for help. However, his body had already been dragged into the river by the four men. His clothes were soaked, and the huge waves were about to engulf him.

A Close Call.

Fortunately, at that critical moment, because it was noon and there were many pedestrians there, Liu's cries were heard by passersby on the wharf. Seeing this scene from afar, they thought that Liu had accidentally fallen into the water while walking on the wooden rafts. Therefore, they called out to nearby boatmen to rush forward and rescue Liu from the water, saving him from drowning. When Liu asked the boatmen if they had seen the four men, they all stared blankly, not knowing what he was talking about.

Turning Pale at the Mention of It.

Soon after, the boatmen sent him to the wharf and handed him over to the police officer on duty, who took him to the First Precinct of the First District. When the precinct chief Yi interrogated him, Liu had calmed down a bit and described the incident in detail, as recorded above. Then, the precinct sent a police officer to escort Liu back to his shop. When the reporter drove to the shop to talk to Liu, he had returned to normal and was sitting at the door, enjoying the breeze. However, when he described the appearance of the four ghosts, his face turned pale, as if he was talking about tigers.

Liu Shufan and Others Appeal Case: Summoning the Property Seller for Questioning.

Prosecutor Questions Three Points.

Zhao Baoshan Still Absent Yesterday.

Former Director of the Postal Savings and Remittances Bureau Liu Shufan, former Manager of the Shanghai Savings and Remittances Branch Ren Sida, and land broker Yang Peichang, Zhao Baoshan, etc., were prosecuted by the Procuratorate of the First Special District District Court for colluding to commit corruption and damage the national treasury. After the first instance sentenced Liu and others to imprisonment, the defendants appealed to the Second Branch of the High Court. Three hearings have already been held, as detailed in previous reports. Yesterday morning, Judge Jiang continued to summon them for questioning. Apart from Zhao Baoshan, who was still absent, Liu, Ren, and Yang, each accompanied by their defense lawyers, turned themselves in. Judge Jiang summoned the Westerner Du Yi to the witness stand to question him about the sale of the Xiafei Road property. According to Du Yi's testimony, the sale of the property was introduced by Yi Sheng and Yang Peichang. The price was 1.2 million. When the deposit was paid, he learned that the buyer was the Savings and Remittances Bureau. Later, the buyer gave the land price in the form of checks. After receiving them, he gave one of the checks worth 150,000 taels to Yang Peichang, Yi Sheng, etc., as commissions. He did not sign it. The remaining checks were all signed by him and deposited in the bank he was dealing with. Regarding the commission, Yang told him that he and Yi Sheng each received 50,000 taels, and the remaining 100,000 taels were obtained by another broker (i.e., Zhao Baoshan). Subsequently, Prosecutor Zhong Qing raised three points: (1) The commission is usually 1% or so. Why was the commission in this case set at a lump sum of 150,000? (2) Was the land price of 1.2 million appropriate at that time, or was there any suspicion of being too high or too low? (3) After the seller received all the checks for the land price, why did he not sign the check for 150,000 taels? What was the reason? He requested to question Du Yi again. Judge Jiang questioned him based on these three points. He then questioned Yan Renshan and securities broker Chen Guangze about the purchase of public bonds on behalf of Yan. Finally, he announced that the hearing would be adjourned to another day.

No Lives Have Been Endangered.

The Results of the Graduation Examinations for Senior and Junior High Schools in Jiangxi Province Have Been Announced ▲ Many Students Failed in Senior and Junior High Schools (Nanchang Correspondence) The graduation examinations for senior and junior high schools in Jiangxi Province this year were completed on June 28th. To facilitate the students' applications for further education, students who were unable to participate due to illness or other reasons were allowed to take a make-up examination once, starting on August 3rd, in accordance with the regulations of the Ministry of Education, after the original school submitted a request and it was approved by the Department of Education. Now, the results of the senior and junior high school graduation examinations have been completely finalized. A total of 47 public and private secondary schools participated in the examinations, with 286 senior high school students. Two hundred and thirteen students passed the examinations and were allowed to graduate. Eighteen students failed in three or more subjects and were required to repeat the grade. As for the school results, Yichun, Xiangshi, and the Second Middle School were the best among the senior high schools, and the private Tongwen, the provincial Jiujiang, and Xiangshi were the best among the junior high schools. The grades of the students and schools have also been announced successively.

Measures for Uniform School Uniforms for Primary and Secondary School Students in This City ▲ Starting This Semester, Students Must Wear Uniforms to Be Admitted to School ▲ New Students and Transfer Students Should Also Follow the Measures to Make Uniforms ▲ Existing Students' Uniforms Must Be Eliminated Within Two Years The Municipal Bureau of Education convened representatives from primary and secondary schools in this city at 2:00 PM yesterday afternoon on the ninth floor of the YMCA at Eight Immortals Bridge to discuss measures for uniform school uniforms for primary and secondary school students. Details are as follows: ▲ Attending Representatives The attendees included Director Pan of the Municipal Bureau of Education, Chen Bai, Zhou Shang, Zhang Yongchun, Shao Rugan, Wang Keyong, Jiao Jihua, Chairman of the National Military Training Association, Luo Lie of the Municipal Boy Scout Council, Shen Xian of the Municipal Sports Ground, and more than 200 representatives from more than 100 schools, including Wusong Xinlu, Wuben, Datong, Guanghua, Daxia, Fushi, Jingye, Zhongxi, Junyi, Zhengshi, Wanzhu, Bide, He'an, Xunyu, Minli, Aiqun, Lida, Zhonghua Vocational School, Puzhong, and Shibei, including Chen Renhe, Cheng Kuanzheng, Xu Zeye, and Gu Yinqian. The Children's Morning Post came to the venue to distribute the Children's Morning Post, and the Zhanghua Woolen Mill and the Shanghai Native Cloth Store sent samples for reference. ▲ Director's Report Director Pan of the Municipal Bureau of Education gave a report, stating, "Some primary and secondary school students in this city already have uniforms, while others do not. The styles of the uniforms of those who already have them are quite inconsistent. The Bureau of Education is now planning to have uniform measures for the uniforms of students in primary and secondary schools within the territory of Shanghai. We can explain the significance of uniform uniforms from two points. First, we acknowledge that students must wear uniforms; without uniforms, they cannot enter school. We want to rectify the academic atmosphere, and wearing uniforms is a method. This is not only a formality, but it is also related to school education. The students' spiritual aspect will also be positively influenced. Second, since we acknowledge that students must wear uniforms, but if the uniforms are not uniform, students will feel very inconvenienced. For example, if a student is in School A this semester and transfers to School B next semester, and the uniforms of School A and School B are completely different, then the student's uniform will only be worn for one semester and will not be applicable, resulting in unnecessary economic losses. Therefore, students must wear uniforms, and the uniforms must have uniform measures. The Bureau of Education has decided on a method based on the student uniform regulations promulgated by the Ministry of Education. We have invited everyone here today to discuss it together." ▲ Discussion of Measures Next, the measures for uniform uniforms were discussed, and the style and color of the uniforms were decided as follows: (A) Boys: High school students' student attire or Zhongshan suit (not yet decided), dark gray for spring and winter, yellow for summer and autumn. Junior high school boy scout uniform, yellow. Elementary school grades implementing boy scout training, boy scout uniform, yellow; the rest are student attire, dark gray for spring and winter, yellow with open collar for summer and autumn. In summer and autumn, single-collar short-sleeved white shirts may be worn. In spring and winter, coats of the same color as the clothing may be worn. Hats: military caps for high school, boy scout hats for boy scout uniforms, melon-skin caps with duckbill brims for elementary school student attire, of the same color as the clothing. Shoes and socks: black, leather or cloth. (B) Girls: High school, dark blue long robes for spring and winter, white shirts and black skirts for summer and autumn. Junior high school girl scout uniform, yellow shirt, black skirt. Elementary school grades implementing boy scout training, girl scout uniform same as junior high school; the rest are student attire, dark blue vest dress for lower grades, white shirt underneath; upper grades same as high school. The color and material samples have also been specified. The regulations will be announced and implemented by the Bureau of Education after revisions, and it has been decided that starting from the first semester of the 23rd academic year, new students and newly admitted transfer students in all primary and secondary schools in this city must make their uniforms in accordance with the uniform measures. Existing students who already have uniforms will be temporarily allowed to use them. Those who do not have them must make them in accordance with the uniform measures. After two years, uniforms for both new and existing students will not be allowed to be different. The rest is omitted.

The Municipal Bureau of Education Orders Peicheng Girls' School to Make Improvements ▲ The Organization of the Board of Directors is Unsound and Must Be Reorganized Within a Time Limit ▲ And Proceed with Registration in Order to Comply with Laws The Municipal Bureau of Education yesterday issued an order to Cao Yunxiang, Chairman of the School Board of Directors, stating, "It was previously reported by Qiao Runwei and other students of the school that the school was not well-managed and was misleading students. After investigation and detailed inspection, it was reported that the school's facilities were indeed lacking in perfection. The following points for improvement are separately instructed: (1) The organization of the school's Board of Directors is very unsound. The seven directors are scattered in various places, and it is difficult to convene a meeting. This means that the board has abandoned its responsibilities for the school, which violates the original purpose of establishing the Board of Directors. It should be reorganized within one month, and the school should select people from the education sector or society in this city who can be truly responsible for the school, submit a list, and report to this bureau for approval to appoint directors and reorganize the board to achieve soundness and promote progress. (2) Primary and secondary schools should be divided immediately, each independent, each with a special name, and each with a principal, so that each can have special responsibilities, but they can be under the guidance and supervision of the same Board of Directors. (3) The administration of primary and secondary schools should have a sound organization. The duties of teaching, academic affairs, and training should be carefully selected and assigned to full-time personnel, each responsible for their duties, in order to assist the principal in handling school affairs. (4) The school should immediately prepare charts and books to handle assessment and statistics, so that the number of students, teaching results, and economic personnel, etc., can all be audited. Education is not an ordinary undertaking, and it is necessary to conduct a detailed review of the reality to know the advantages and disadvantages and refer to improvements. The school has been deficient in this in the past. (5) There should be concrete measures for training and managing students, and rules should be established so that students can abide by them. Memorial week should be held earnestly. (6) The curriculum set by the school still follows past habits, and there are many discrepancies between the assessment and the standards of the curriculum issued by the Ministry of Education. Efforts should be made to improve it, and Party principles or civics courses should be added. The time for English should be reduced, and attention should be paid to the balance of moral, intellectual, physical, and group education to avoid bias and prevent abuses. (7) The school's senior high school business courses do not meet the regulations and should be canceled immediately. (8) The school's classification of new students is based solely on the entrance examination, and it has never investigated the qualifications of students and student photos, etc., which often leads to students skipping grades. Even the same student can often change their name and retake the exam, thereby skipping grades. This not only destroys the academic system, but also cultivates the psychology of young people seeking advancement by chance. In the future, it must be thoroughly reformed. (9) The school has been established for nine years, but it has not yet been registered, which has a great impact on the future of students. It should proceed with registration as soon as possible in order to comply with laws." The chairman of the school's Board of Directors should supervise the principal to earnestly comply with the above points and make improvements as soon as possible, and report the handling situation for verification without delay. This order is also to inform the students of the school about the improvement situation. The disturbances have been quelled.

Aurora University Expands Chemistry Laboratory The College of Science and Engineering of Aurora University has gradually developed and made progress in recent years. Recently, the chemistry laboratory has been expanded due to its small size and insufficient use. The old site has been rebuilt into a large building, which will be completed soon. The new building is 35 meters long and 12 meters wide, divided into two floors. The lower floor is for general chemistry laboratories, specially for the use of students in the first two years of the chemistry department. The rooms are quite spacious. The upper floor is for industrial chemistry, organic chemistry, and biochemistry laboratories. There are also four small laboratories for professors to conduct individual research. The school has recently collected many sets of mineral specimens from China, France, Russia, and other countries and has opened a special room for their collection. In addition, there are large lecture halls, balance rooms, dark rooms, instrument rooms, and medicine rooms, all connected to the laboratory, so that transportation is convenient. Therefore, the entire building is like a small chemical research institute. It is said that students in the chemistry department of the school, after completing four years of study and graduating, will be able to make considerable contributions to the various chemical industries that are emerging in the country.

Therefore, the total number of new students this time is expected to exceed the first examination, but the number of admissions is only 90, so the level of the admitted students must be very excellent. In addition, the 28th of this month is the opening date of the school. The important teachers of each department have arrived at the school, and the staff of the three departments of academic affairs, training, and student affairs are busy formulating progress schedules and planning students' extracurricular activities.

Jingye Middle School Enrolls Students The Municipal Jingye Middle School has been vigorously rectifying and making rapid progress in recent years. In the last semester, the two-year construction plan completed the school building equipment, and the atmosphere was renewed. In addition, the results of this year's conference examination were the best in the city, and the reputation was greatly enhanced. Those who applied for the make-up examination were extremely enthusiastic, breaking previous records. It is learned that the second batch of new students will be announced in the newspaper today.

Kunfan Girls' Middle School Begins Classes Kunfan Girls' Middle School on Meibai Road has a pure and simple school spirit and perfect equipment. The school's training and education policies for this academic year have been carefully planned and implemented. The school officially started classes yesterday, with more than 500 new and old students attending. The number of people requesting registration is still endless. In order to meet the requirements of parents, the enrollment committee convened a temporary meeting yesterday and decided to add classrooms and expand the number of students by 40, which will be closed as soon as it is full and will not be accommodated any further.

Guangxia Middle School Scheduled to Open The Guangxia Middle School on Xinzha Road has always been known for its strict management and education. The graduates of previous sessions have mostly been admitted to famous universities and served the community in large numbers. Dr. Lu Xirong, the principal of the school, has concrete plans for the administration of the next semester, paying special attention to the employment problems of graduates. The number of applicants has been unusually enthusiastic in recent days. In order to meet the requirements of visitors from all sides, another new student examination will be held on the 29th of this month, and registration will begin on September 1st.

Sports News Ministry of Education Orders Improvement of Physical Education Key Points for Colleges and Above (2) (XIII) Minguo College The points that need to be improved in the college's physical education are summarized as follows: (1) The personnel responsible for the college's physical education are all part-time, and the work efficiency is greatly affected. In the future, full-time teachers should be rehired to be responsible for guidance, so that the college's physical education work can be promoted. (2) Regarding the college's physical education specialty, (1) there are too many part-time teachers, and full-time teachers should be rehired as much as possible to facilitate teaching; (2) the funding is mixed with the college's physical education funding, which is also inappropriate. In the future, separate budgets should be established to develop the system; (3) it is not appropriate for five girls to take classes with boys, as their physical strength is different and their interests are not the same. In the future, the department should immediately stop recruiting girls, and the existing girls should be allowed to transfer to other schools; (4) the equipment is not sufficient and should be added as soon as possible. The track and field ground is too empty and has no runway, and should also be improved as soon as possible; (5) students' notes are not clear enough and should be improved.

B Tianjin (XIV) Nankai University The school has always attached great importance to physical education, and has been carefully planned by the responsible personnel of physical education. After ten years of research and improvement, there have been significant achievements. In the future, efforts should continue to be made to increase physical education funding and enrich physical education equipment to seek further progress. The proposed construction of a gymnasium and swimming pool in the near future is a very important plan and should be carried out as soon as possible and completed as soon as possible. (XV) Beiyang Institute of Technology The personnel responsible for physical education in the college are working hard to promote universal activities, which is very good. However, physical education teachers still need to be rehired, and although physical education equipment is still sufficient, the track and field ground must also be improved. The college's regulations on students' selection of sports time and the measures to eliminate absenteeism are very good, but how to guide and test students when participating in sports has not been clearly stipulated. You can refer to the methods established by Tsinghua, Nankai, Wuhan, and other schools and consider the college's situation to formulate standards to facilitate the process. (XVI) Women's Normal College The college's physical education organization is still complete, and the promotion of physical education can also be carried out step by step. It is especially valuable that ordinary physical education can be promoted universally. However, the college's outdoor sports ground is insufficient and must be increased. In addition, there are too few full-time teachers in the college's physical education specialty, and most of the students' notes are not very detailed and should be improved. The college's extracurricular rhythmic exercises should also be promoted. (XVII) Hebei Institute of Technology The college has made great efforts to promote physical education, and students are very interested in physical education. Extracurricular activities can also be promoted seriously and attention should be paid to popularization. However, physical education personnel still need to be rehired appropriately to facilitate the process. In addition, the college's various physical education equipment is clean and suitable, but the track and field runway should be expanded to make it more perfect. (XVIII) Hebei College of Law and Commerce The college's proposed future physical education plan, the first item regarding the definition of goals, is too empty, and equipment should be added when the second item of adding disciplines is implemented. The third item of implementation measures is more important and should be implemented as soon as possible. In addition, the college's track and field runway should be expanded to facilitate teaching. (XIX) Tianjin Institute of Industry and Commerce The college's physical education teachers are all part-time, and most of the physical education facilities are the responsibility of the students themselves, which is not appropriate. Specialized talents should be rehired immediately to be responsible for planning and actively guiding. Students pay a physical education fee of six yuan each year, which is too much and should be reduced appropriately. In addition, the funding should be used exclusively for adding equipment, and the salaries of teachers should be paid from the school's funding.

C Baoding (XX) Hebei Agricultural College The college's physical education facilities are still serious, and it attaches great importance to promoting our country's inherent sports games and forcing students to participate in outdoor sports after class, which is very good. However, forced sports can only be implemented temporarily, and in the future, it should be actively developed from the aspects of organization and interest to cultivate students' habit of automatically participating in sports activities. In addition, the college's physical education equipment is still sufficient, but the track and field ground is too small and should be expanded as soon as possible to make it suitable. The college's plan to build a gymnasium is indeed an important plan and should be realized as soon as possible. The completion of this building will not only greatly benefit the development of physical education for students in the college, but also specify a time and make it public to students and the public in the area within the possible range in the future, which will definitely have considerable assistance in the development of physical education in the community. (XXI) Hebei Medical College The college's physical education funding should be determined to a considerable amount to facilitate facilities. Extracurricular physical education activities should appropriately advance the class time to give students sufficient opportunities to participate. Female physical education also needs to rehire teachers to be responsible for guidance. In addition, the college's proposed construction of an outdoor swimming pool should be realized as soon as possible.

D Kaifeng (XXII) Henan University The college's physical education should be listed as a compulsory subject as soon as possible, and attention should be paid to the universal participation of all students in extracurricular activities. Female physical education should be rehired to guide teachers to facilitate teaching. The college holds morning exercises every day, which has achieved results, but the content of the teaching materials still needs to be improved. In addition, the college's agricultural college physical education teachers do not often come to the college, and the work efficiency is very low. The college's physical education director should be responsible for effectively improving it.

(E Wuhan) (XXIII) Wuhan University The college's regulations on physical education facilities are very strict, such as the scoring method of physical education results and the physical education pass standards, which are sufficient to arouse students' efforts in physical education and should be implemented as soon as possible. However, the physical education pass standards must be increased at any time based on the students' physical education progress. The college's physical education courses are scheduled after 4:00 PM, which is too short and should be appropriately advanced to facilitate students' participation. The construction of gymnasiums and swimming pools is urgently needed and should be started as soon as possible. (XXIV) Wuchang Huazhong University Students in the college have always been very interested in physical education, but recently, the efficiency of the college's physical education facilities has been reduced due to the lack of a dedicated person responsible for them. In the future, special personnel should be rehired to be responsible for the facilities. The college's physical education equipment is still sufficient, but the track and field runway should be improved, and the unfinished runway in the gymnasium should also be completed as soon as possible. In addition, track and field sports are the foundation of various sports, and this subject should be added to the physical education curriculum for study. (XXV) Wuchang Zhonghua University The college's physical education administrative organization is too complicated and should be simplified to make it easier to implement and effective. Physical education teachers should be rehired with specialized knowledge and experience, and teachers should be rehired for women to provide guidance. In addition, the college's equipment is not sufficient, and although it has been added over the years, most of them are consumables. In the future, efforts should be made to enrich fixed equipment. The planned construction of sports grounds and gymnasiums is very important and should be realized as soon as possible. Other physical education departments should be added, physical education research associations should be established, and physical education libraries should be set up, which should not be opened until there are sufficient teachers and equipment and approved by the Ministry of Education. (XXVI) Hubei Institute of Education The college is still able to pay attention to students' physical education, and the morning exercise method is also considered serious. However, there is only one hour of physical education course per week, which is too little and should be increased appropriately. The content of the morning exercise teaching materials must be changed from time to time to avoid being rigid and to increase students' interest. In addition, the planned construction of tennis courts in the college and the addition of various equipment in the gymnasium is an important plan and should be realized as soon as possible. However, indoor equipment should not be limited to volleyball and gymnastics, and other ball sports should also be given the same attention.

F Changsha (XXVII) Hunan University The college has been able to add physical education venues in recent years, but the construction of gymnasiums and swimming pools, and the addition of physical education courses in each department, are all important plans and should be realized as soon as possible. In terms of organization, a physical education department should be added, with one physical education director to preside over planning, and physical education teachers and female instructors should be added appropriately to facilitate the process. (XXVIII) Xiangya Medical College The college's physical education teachers are part-time, which is not appropriate. In the future, specialized talents should be rehired immediately to be responsible for the facilities. The organization should also be improved. The physical education activities of the Student Physical Education Association and various grade associations should be actively guided by the school's physical education personnel to facilitate development.

G Anqing (XXIX) Anhui University The college's physical education funding has not been determined, and one physical education teacher is also insufficient for the number of assignments. A considerable amount of funds should be determined and instructors should be rehired to facilitate the process. In addition, the college's physical education venues are mostly simple, and in the future, when building new school buildings, efforts must be made to realize the plan to expand physical education equipment.

Commercial News, Securities, and Departure from the Norm in the Bond Market

Market Prices Rise and Fall in the Blink of an Eye

Nearly 40 Million in Transactions Across Three Sessions

Yesterday, the Shanghai Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange experienced extremely peculiar market trends, with ups and downs occurring rapidly, giving one a dizzying feeling. Rumors also rose and fell unpredictably, demonstrating the public's bewilderment and unease. In reality, these rumors were mostly unfounded, but it is true that many bulls in the market took the opportunity to sell at high prices. Therefore, market prices rose and fell very quickly. This kind of situation is also due to the approaching settlement date. The future trend will likely involve further fluctuations. Yesterday's trading involved three sessions, and the market did not close until after 7 PM, which shows the enthusiasm of the trading. This abnormal development is still in its early stages. At the opening yesterday, confidence was strong, and prices generally tended to rise, from several cents to over a dollar. However, starting with the Unified Tax forward contracts, the market weakened again, falling by a few cents to half a dollar. The trends before and after this point moved in opposite directions, and confidence shifted downward again. In the second session, prices plummeted by several cents to as much as $1.60, indicating that bulls were selling off to save themselves. In the afternoon, paper contracts were traded in one session, which started close to 6 PM. Bulls temporarily stopped selling, and various groups showed signs of pushing prices up, leading to another round of rising prices, up around one dollar. The speed of the changes and the strangeness of the rises and falls were truly abnormal. This phenomenon is likely to continue for the next few days. The market price results showed mixed rises and falls, with the first twenty contracts or so doing slightly better, around two or three cents, while most others were down by three, five, or six cents. The total transaction volume remained in the range of 40 million yuan. Due to the late hour, detailed listings could not be provided. New York Agricultural District Railroad Stocks Perform Strongly

A report from New Fown Yew Hang states that yesterday (the 21st), the market sentiment on the New York Stock Exchange turned strong, with agricultural district railroad stocks being particularly strong. Sugar stocks rose due to favorable news about the Cuban trade agreement. Stocks of agricultural implements, mail-order stores, and fertilizers also rose as grain prices improved. Trading on the small exchange was quiet, but the market was also firm due to the rise in mining stocks. The bond market initially wavered due to the weakness of U.S. government bonds but then rebounded quickly, with uneven movements. The Chicago wheat market saw active trading by retail investors, with brokers' liquidations being absorbed by the public. The total daily transaction volume was 580,000 shares. Financial Exchange Rates Remain Firm, Gold Prices Continue to Fall by $2.50

--Midday Trading Hovered Around the $50 Mark--

Although sentiment in the gold market is still stable, there have been rumors recently that banks will cooperate to lower exchange rates, hoping to narrow the gap between domestic and foreign exchange rates and prevent the outflow of silver. The exchange market is unusually loose, and the gold market is linked to arbitrage, so sellers are more active. Yesterday, the market continued to fall. In the morning, overseas silver markets in both the UK and the US were flat. The price of raw gold in London fell by half a penny, and exchange rates rose slightly. American cotton rose by 14 points, American wheat rose by 6.25, and stocks also rose by over $2. The commodity market opened flat, but gold prices fell immediately after pre-market trading, mainly because the exchange market was loose and banks had no appetite for buying. After the opening, prices were still flat, but since banks remained resistant to buying, sellers became more aggressive and broke through the $50 mark. Although buyers came in to take advantage of the lower prices, the market remained weak due to the sudden widening of HSBC's exchange rate quotes. However, the underlying sentiment was still stable, and public sentiment was calm. After that, the market sought a balance, and gold prices entered a period of fluctuation. The market remained flat for a long time. Later, the banks' appetite for selling decreased slightly, and Chinese merchants continued to make small purchases, gradually pushing prices above $50. There were also rumors that the Central Bank was opening spot trading, which boosted buying interest among large investors, and domestic trading also tightened slightly and rose. However, banks were still willing to sell, and there was still a pullback. The midday close was relatively flat. The decline was still due to the loose exchange market, and the outlook still involves fluctuations. The price of gold was approximately 12 yuan. The midday market situation is recorded below:

The morning opening was $550.20, down $3.10 from the previous close. Commodities opened at 6 points. The morning opening exchange rates for near-term sales were 1 shilling 4.6875 pence for British pounds and 35.3125 yuan for US dollars. Although Wing Lei Shiu Fung Cheong advanced to $1.20, Citibank sold October US dollars at half a point, to 56.25, Yuan Yick, Heng Yu, Ching Cheong, Tai Tak, and Shing Hong sold, breaking through the $50 mark, retreating to $48.20. Tai Fat and Wing King Yu advanced to over $50, but Great Britain and Citibank sold November US dollars at 68.75, Yuan Cheong, Ping Ting Cheong sold contracts, falling again to $8.50. Although Fook Hing, Wing Yick, Shing Shun, Yue Kun Cheong Cheong advanced to over $9, the price fell to $8 due to the news that HSBC had raised its rates by 125 points for pounds and 25 points for US dollars, and the domestic market was loose. Major investors such as Fook Tai Heng, Ping Shing, Tai Fat, Wing Tai Tak Cheong, and Shiu Fung Cheong all sold. Fook Hing, Wing Kun Cheong Cheong, Shiu Fung Cheong, Tai Fat, and Wing took advantage of the low prices to buy, HSBC bought October US dollars at 56.25, rising to $9.30. Yuan Yick, Yee Fung, Wing Chun Yuen, Wing Shang still had selling interest, but since Tai Hing, Wing Yick Shing, Man Hing, Heng Hing were buying contracts, the price fluctuated around $9, which was extremely flat. Later, with the rumors that the Central Bank was opening spot trading, Tai Hing, Wing Heng Yu, Tai Tak Cheong, Yuan Mao, Wing Yuan Fung, Wing Wai Cheung, Ting Hong commodities all bought, and October US dollars at half a point were difficult to settle, breaking through the $50 mark, rising to $51.50. Fook Yu, Tung Tai Cheong Yuen Hing sold out, and prices fell. Banks also sold October US dollars at half a point, retreating to zero points. However, because public sentiment was still stable, Yuan Mao, Wing Shun Mao took advantage of the low prices to maintain the position, and it was still possible to pull the price up. After entering the market, October US dollars at half a point were still difficult to settle, Yuan Heng, Tai Tak Cheong, Kun Cheong Cheong, Yu King Wing, etc. bought aggressively, and the price rose again to $1.90. Retail investors sold at high prices, and although there were buyers, prices still fell slightly. The midday close was $950.80, and commodities were priced at the same level. After the close, the market initially seemed weak, but because Fook Hing, Wing Ting Cheong all had buying interest, the market was calm. The highest price during the midday trading was $951.90, and the lowest was $948, a fluctuation of $3.90. The result was a decrease of $2.50 from the previous close.

The closing price was based on HSBC's exchange rate for US dollars, which rose by 25 points to $35, resulting in a standard gold price of $988, which was strong. According to the closing price, the premium was approximately $38, which was weak, a decrease of $4 from the previous close. The registered prices for this month were $957, $953 for September, and $951 for October. The morning make-up water was $957. The price of gold was approximately $962.20, approximately $12 more. Tianjin goods were discounted to void, but upon arrival, they were still slightly higher than the port price. There was a lack of buyers in the market, and the approximate purchase price for Tianjin goods was $13 more. The swap market turned firm, with Dalian groups Wan Hing and Shun Lee posting bids, which were bought by Ting Tai, Ting Cheong, and Fook Cheong, totaling approximately 200 contracts, all at $1.50. Later, Fook Cheong was willing to buy, and Yick Shing sold 126 contracts to Heng Yu for $1.20. The final price was approximately $1. It was reported that the Central Bank had opened spot trading at a price of approximately $951, which was handled by bull companies. September contracts were transferred from Fook Hing Wing to Fook Cheong, 392 contracts, priced at $955.50. In addition, there were also transfers for October contracts. The number of contracts for this month and September has gradually decreased. As of today, only 21 contracts remain for this month, with Fook Cheong being the buyer and Tai Shun being the seller.

Trading in the market was flat. Banks' Selling Intentions Not Urgent, Exchange Market is Clearly and Obscurely Loose

According to foreign telegrams yesterday, both London large contracts and American banks were flat, raw gold in London decreased by half a penny, the British pound against the US dollar did not change, the US dollar against the British pound increased by 3.75, the British pound against the French franc decreased by 13 points, and the US dollar against the French franc increased by 75 points. The morning opening exchange market was the same as the previous close, with near-term selling prices of 1 shilling 4.625 pence for British pounds and 35.25 yuan for US dollars. The market was hard after opening because there were rumors recently that banks will lower exchange rates, so Chinese merchants are not willing to make small purchases easily, banks are very willing to sell, and it is loose after the opening. The opening of HSBC’s exchange rates showed that the British pound increased by 125 points and the US dollar increased by 25 points, which was the hardest at this time. After entering the market, Chinese merchants took advantage of the low prices to make purchases, and banks also made transactions, so the process was flat. The gold market suddenly had many buyers, gold prices rose, and Chinese merchants’ buying intentions were then stronger, which was slightly tight, but banks provided them from time to time, but the selling intentions were more inactive.

Yarn and Cotton Yarn Futures Market: Selling Becomes Stronger in the Afternoon

However, there were no major short sellers, and the bulls among the money houses had not yet released their positions, so the market sentiment was still flat. This month's yarn fell by another 1.5 yuan.

In the morning session for standard yarn, despite rising American cotton prices, the price of yarn for this month fell due to sufficient supply for delivery, which exerted downward pressure. Distant months were also affected. A certain factory was also selling short, and the issue of money houses taking delivery was still under consideration. As a result, prices for all months rose and fell by 0.2, 0.3, and 0.7 cents. In the afternoon, it was heard that spot yarn sales were not smooth, and rumors in the market were rampant. Public bonds fell sharply, and the opening situation was severe, with prices for all months falling by 0.7 and 0.8 cents. However, the selling pressure did not become particularly strong until the second and third sessions. As a result, prices for all months fell again by 0.8, 0.9 cents to 1.12 yuan. Respecting the Diplomatic War Between Japan and the Soviet Union 34

The Buying and Selling of the Chinese Eastern Railway: After the Japanese Foreign Minister declined mediation, the puppet state of Manchukuo condemned the Soviet Union for its lack of sincerity. Hachiro Arita then left Tokyo to return to Manchuria, and the so-called conference fell back into a stalemate. This kind of stalemate was expected by us long ago and is not a surprise. From the very beginning of the negotiations, it was obvious that the Soviet Union wanted to sell the railway in exchange for temporary peace, and the Japanese were willing to buy it to deal with the temporary situation. The lack of sincerity in their negotiations was apparent from the start. The three northeastern provinces were originally part of our country's territory. With Japan and the Soviet Union using them as a buffer, direct conflict was less likely to occur, and Far Eastern peace had an additional layer of protection. However, after the Japanese army completely occupied our Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang provinces, Japan and the Soviet Union found themselves in a situation of constant close contact. There was no room to avoid conflict. The greatest effect of diplomacy was merely to use clever means to slightly delay the inevitable. For example, in the current dispute over the price of the Eastern Railway, the Soviet Union's asking price gradually decreased from 250 million gold rubles (equivalent to 625 million Japanese yen) to 160 million Japanese yen. The Japanese side, on the other hand, increased their initial counteroffer of 50 million Japanese yen to the current 120 million yen after Hirota's negotiation. On the surface, the gap between the two sides seems to have narrowed, but in reality, the confrontational situation has intensified. This is because the Soviet Union's desire to exchange the Chinese Eastern Railway for peace is not genuine, and the Japanese side only wants to use these negotiations to buy time to prepare its military strength. The conference is merely a diplomatic formality, so how can there be any hope of success?

On the very day the conference stalled, more than 20 Russian employees of the Eastern Railway were arrested on suspicion of certain offenses. This further aroused the Soviet Union's displeasure, and they accused Japan and Manchukuo of being barbaric. Japan and Manchukuo retorted, accusing the Soviet Union of intentionally disrupting the railway administration. The negotiations became increasingly dangerous. The diplomatic war of words between the two sides broke out again, with each side shifting responsibility to imply that if a break occurred as a result, the responsibility would lie with the other party and not themselves. The tension of the situation is all the more conceivable. However, Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota suddenly issued a statement saying that the door to negotiations was not closed. Could it be that there is still genuine sincerity in the negotiations? It is merely that Hirota wants to have Manchukuo appear at the forefront while he hides behind the scenes. If the negotiations are indeed successful, it can raise the status of the puppet regime, and Hirota can still maintain his original power to issue commands. The puppet regime's gains are no different from Japan's gains. Even if the stalemate expands, the Chinese Eastern Railway is already in the hands of the Japanese army, and they can easily use cunning tactics to create room for maneuver and employ their double-dealing diplomatic skills.

Amidst this tense situation between the two sides, Moscow is deploying troops, and the situation on the Jilin-Heilongjiang border is very urgent. Along the Ussuri River, the strengthening of military defenses and preparedness is even stricter. After the Soviet railway employees were arrested, it was rumored that the Soviet Union was organizing groups of railway employees, women, and children to return to their country by train. In the Harbin area, diplomatic personnel are being secretly monitored. All kinds of rumors are spreading everywhere, which only increases the seriousness of the problem. On the Japanese side, in addition to strongly criticizing the Soviet authorities for their lack of sincerity in diplomatic words, they are intensifying their military preparations. Furthermore, at this time, they have completed their so-called Japan-(Manchukuo) liaison transportation plan, with the sea and land route from Tokyo via Tsuruga, Chongjin, and Guomen to Changchun successfully operating. They admit that this line has great military value, as troops in (Manchukuo) can be steadily and quickly transported by land, and a double-ring blockade of Vladivostok can be achieved at sea. The air force stationed in the four northeastern provinces will soon hold large-scale exercises. Although this may be a pre-scheduled procedure, it undeniably contains a very strong deterrent nature.

Based on this, if we speculate on how events will unfold, the Japanese side has already declared that its policy toward the Soviet Union will change from moderate to aggressive. Initially, they plan to thoroughly demand the reorganization of the Chinese Eastern Railway, and based on the Sino-Russian and Feng-Russian agreements, authority must be divided and finances must be jointly managed. This is the determined diplomatic approach. Arita will also start to implement this immediately. If the Soviet Union cannot agree, then the puppet state of Manchukuo will rely on the Japan-(Manchukuo) military agreement to jointly defend. In other words, they will seize the Chinese Eastern Railway by force. Therefore, from a factual perspective, there is a fear of crisis at any moment in the Jilin-Heilongjiang border and various parts of eastern Siberia. The war of public opinion between Tokyo and Moscow has gradually unfolded and is more intense than ever before. After the war of words, each side has its own unique military strength to rely on. If there is no solution, the only outcome will be a competition of strength. However, at present, they are still shifting responsibility to each other and seeking the judgment of world opinion based on notions such as sincerity and law. Until both sides complete their military preparations, the so-called diplomatic war of words will still be lively for a while.

More Russian Employees Arrested 37

The Possibility of War Between Japan and Russia is Imminent (Harbin) Today, another 17 or 18 Soviet Russian employees of the eastern section of the Chinese Eastern Railway were arrested by (Manchukuo) police at the director's office on suspicion of being Soviet spies. Observers here view the overall situation as extremely precarious. If the Soviet Union or (Manchukuo) engages in intimidating demonstrations on the border, conducts military exercises, or moves large numbers of troops, it will be enough to trigger an incident. Both countries are now concerned about sudden attacks and aerial bombardments. (20th Reuters) (Tokyo) Today, all newspapers commented on the transfer negotiations of the Chinese Eastern Railway. With the exception of the Hochi Shimbun, they all urged the Soviet Russian government to reconsider its attitude. The Hochi Shimbun advised the Russian and Japanese governments not to engage in a war of words. The Asahi Shimbun stated that (Manchukuo)'s offer, including the severance pay for Soviet Russian employees, totaled 150 million Japanese yen, while Soviet Russia was asking for 190 million Japanese yen. Judging from the large difference in the initial conditions of the Russian-(Manchukuo) negotiations, the distance between the two sides today is not significant. (22nd Reuters)

Manchukuo Makes a Cookie-Cutter Statement Regarding the Chinese Eastern Railway 38

(Changchun) The (Manchukuo Foreign Ministry) issued a statement at 1:00 PM on the 22nd to clarify its attitude regarding the negotiations for the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway. The statement detailed the course of the negotiations and stated that the Eastern Railway was a legacy of Russian imperialism and that the Soviet Union had repeatedly declared its intention to abandon it. The railway was originally a joint enterprise managed by both Manchu and Soviet countries and was by no means the exclusive property of the Soviet Union. Finally, regarding the issue of the arrest of Soviet Russian employees of the Chinese Eastern Railway, it strongly asserted the following: (Manchukuo)'s arrest of Soviet Russian employees of the Chinese Eastern Railway was because some of these employees were colluding with righteous armies to disrupt public order within (Manchukuo), especially by repeatedly destroying railways and derailing military trains, causing numerous casualties. Therefore, in order to prevent general red terror, they had no choice but to take self-defense measures. This has no connection to the negotiations of the Chinese Eastern Railway. It is obvious that the Soviet government deliberately combines these two cases into one, which must be regarded as an attempt to restrain the natural measures of the (Manchukuo government). (20th Japanese Alliance)

Japanese Provocation Against Russia 39

Harmful to World Peace - The Views of the French Press (Paris) The provocative actions of Japan and Manchukuo against the Soviet Union are increasingly provoking sharp criticism from the French press. Various newspapers point out that the actions of Japan and Manchukuo not only threaten the Soviet-Japanese border but are even harmful to world peace. The French press often claims that the actions of the Japanese side are directly harmful to France, whether in terms of French interests in Asia or in terms of the serious consequences that would arise if the conflict in Asia were to spread to Europe. More and more people are now expressing this view. Le Temps published a lengthy article attacking the fabrication of news and provocative rumors by Japan and Manchukuo. It stated, "(These statements only seek to exacerbate the systematic and deliberate distortion of facts, the purpose of which is to provide arguments against Soviet Russia's accession to the League of Nations and the conclusion of mutual assistance pacts.)" The newspaper pointed out that the center of anti-Soviet propaganda is in Harbin, where all kinds of mutually contradictory news are being spread in the hope of causing incidents in Manchuria or even abroad. Le Temps emphasized that White Russians residing in France are helping to spread these provocative rumors and stated that there is currently a secret anti-Soviet society of a terrorist nature. Le Siècle mentioned the suspected anti-Soviet plans of Japan and Germany, as well as the Soviet government's repeatedly tested spirit of peace, and said that only the Soviet Union would never retreat before any aggressor. French military authorities deeply believe that the Red Army will surely make aggressors regret their adventurous actions. La République stated, "(We cannot be indifferent to the fate of our friend, the Soviet Union. It is admirable that the Soviet Union can be so resolute in the face of constant troubles.)" (21st TASS)

Japan Builds a Powerful Broadcasting Station 41

To Facilitate Foreign Propaganda - Costing 3 Million Yen (Tokyo) Currently, countries around the world are competing to build high-power radio broadcasting stations. China's Nanjing station with 75 kilowatts, Changsha's station with 125 kilowatts, and Soviet Russia's Khabarovsk station with 130 kilowatts are all considered powerful broadcasting stations. Japan, in the midst of this, has decided to control radio waves and build a high-power broadcasting station to use for foreign propaganda in times of emergency. The Japan Broadcasting Corporation (NHK) has established a plan and applied for its establishment. As a result, it officially received permission from the Ministry of Communications on the 21st. According to the plan, using this year's temporary budget of 3 million yen, the current 10-kilowatt machinery of the first and second broadcasting stations will be replaced with 150-kilowatt machinery. Whether day or night, its sound can be received by ordinary receivers in China, Manchuria, and Siberia. The NHK also plans to build 100-kilowatt broadcasting stations in Osaka and Kyushu in 1936 in order to overcome the era of difficult radio wave reception. (22nd Japanese Alliance)
